Siamese Revolution Completed Overnight 87

The Radical Party, United with the Navy and Army, Occupies the Capital Silently. The Conservative Government is Overthrown. National News Agency's Bangkok Dispatch on the 21st: Siamese radicals, taking advantage of the King's absence from the capital this morning, and with the help of naval and army personnel, suddenly occupied the capital and arrested conservative leaders. Before the King returns to the capital, the government is temporarily managed by military leaders. This bloodless revolution is like the revolution of June 24th last year, without firing a shot or injuring anyone. Colonel Phraya Phaholphonphayuhasena, the Army Commander-in-Chief, resigned yesterday. After midnight, he suddenly led troops to surround the Royal Palace and arrested Prince Manopakon Nitithat, the President of the State Council, Phraya Sri Sena, the Minister of Foreign Affairs, and Phraya Thepharit Phanuphandhu, the Minister of Defense. Later, Prince Manopakon Nitithat resigned and was temporarily replaced by Colonel Phraya Phaholphonphayuhasena, awaiting the King's return from the Huai Hin Summer Palace for disposition. The most recent cause of the revolution was that the State Council failed to adopt the radical economic plan proposed by the former Chairman, Pridi Banomyong, two months ago. Subsequently, the State Council and the National Assembly were accused of having communist inclinations and were dissolved on April 1st, and the power was completely taken over by conservatives who formed another State Council with Prince Manopakon Nitithat as its head. Pridi Banomyong immediately fled to Europe, and the radicals secretly conspired with Colonel Phraya Phaholphonphayuhasena to launch a revolution, which lasted fifty days, resulting in today's uprising. Pridi and Phraya were both leaders of the revolution of June last year. Today's revolution was not only bloodless, but also completely silent. The Navy and Army had secretly made thorough arrangements. Upon a command, they immediately quietly marched to the designated locations. The people initially heard nothing. When they woke up this morning, they suddenly saw troops surrounding the government offices and realized that the government had undergone another change.

Furthermore, observing the situation of the revolution, one gets the impression that the Siamese King knew about it in advance and used the excuse of going to the Huai Hin Summer Palace. However, in any case, it is expected that the Siamese King will certainly comply with the requests of the radicals, issue new orders, and implement new measures. However, the extensive powers granted to him by the constitution are likely to be slightly reduced after this revolution. As for the conservatives, it is unlikely that they will be able to carry out a resistance movement. It is expected that those arrested will be released as civilians after things are settled.

National News Agency's Bangkok Dispatch on the 21st: Colonel Phraya Phaholphonphayuhasena, the temporary dictator of Siam, has asked the King on behalf of the radicals to immediately convene the National Assembly and the State Council dissolved on April 1st and to reinstate Pridi Banomyong and other radicals who were dismissed at the same time. Pridi is currently in France, but the radicals all want him to return to the country and take charge of the government. It is said that if Pridi's faction can regain power and implement its radical plan to help farmers, then Pridi will immediately return to Siam. However, Pridi himself may not want to serve as Chairman of the State Council again. According to a radical leader today, Pridi does not want to be an official, but only wants to see his economic plan effectively implemented. As for his plan, it is a compromise between democracy and communism. Currently, Bangkok is peaceful and stable. Only naval and army soldiers are patrolling the streets. Newspapers and telegrams are all subject to strict inspection.

Bangkok Dispatch on the 21st: Yesterday's coup was peaceful. It was merely a change in the government's leadership and had nothing to do with the Siamese King's position. The one in charge this time was Phraya Phaholphonphayuhasena, the Commander-in-Chief of the Siamese Navy and Army. Phraya had previously carried out the first revolution, limiting the authority of the Siamese King. This time, he overthrew the old Executive Council and announced that he would convene a people's assembly to conform to the constitution. At the same time, he telegraphed the Siamese King, who was taking a summer retreat in Huai Hin, informing him that the Navy, Army, and people supported the King, so they took this action, the purpose of which was to reorganize the Executive Council. The current Siamese King, now thirty-nine years old, ascended the throne in 1925. After the political system was changed to a constitutional monarchy last year, a provisional constitution was promulgated in June, stipulating that the supreme power belonged to the people and that the monarch was the head of state. The executive power was exercised by a fifteen-member committee. It also stipulated that a parliament should be convened, consisting of seventy members, half appointed and half elected. This year, the Siamese King dissolved parliament in April on the pretext of preventing the spread of communism and established another Executive Council to await the election of a new parliament. Phraya Phaholphonphayuhasena advocated the immediate convening of parliament and was dissatisfied with this transitional arrangement, so there was a second revolution today.

Soviet Russia Rectifies the Rule of Law 88

Establishes a Ministry of Justice to Supervise the Secret Police. National News Agency's Moscow Dispatch on the 21st: The Soviet Russian government, in view of the fact that the secret political police and the courts of first instance often abuse police power or judicial power and that judgments are unfair, announced today the establishment of a Ministry of Justice with broad supervisory powers and the power to review cases at any time, as well as the power to comment on whether the activities of the secret political police are legal and justified.

New York Banks Oppose

Germany Suspends Debt Payments 89

Reuters' New York Dispatch on the 21st: Today, various New York banks telegraphed Dr. Schacht, the President of the Deutsche Bank, stating that the method of suspending all debts owed to Germany before July 1931 was inappropriate, unfair, and harmful to Germany's credit. The suspension order was announced on June 8th. According to Schacht, the reason for this move was entirely due to the current financial panic in Germany, and the reason for this panic was caused by the banking crisis in 1931. The suspension order affects the principal and interest of German debt amounting to 865,000,000 pounds.

The Waters of the Yangtze River in Wuhan Continue to Rise Sharply 90

The Jinshui New Dam Collapses. The Dike on the Yangtze River in Wuchang Cracks. All Members of the Provincial Government Inspect the Wutai Gate. The Flood Control Dike in Hankou is Closed. The Japanese Concession is Flooded. A Hankou dispatch reports that it has been raining continuously for days, and the Yangtze River is rising sharply. In the past two days, the weather has cleared, and it was thought that heaven was blessing our people and that the water level could gradually stabilize. Unexpectedly, the floods are torrential and are coming even more fiercely. On the 20th, the water level rose sharply by one foot in one day, reaching 44 feet and one inch, which is five feet and seven inches higher than the water level of 38 feet and four inches on the same day in the 20th year (of the Republic) and more than one zhang higher than the water level of 33 feet and two inches in the 21st year. Currently, the counties along the Yangtze River are gradually becoming disaster areas. There is water leakage at the Wutai Gate in Wuchang, the Jinshui Dam has collapsed, the dike on the Yangtze River in Taizijie has cracked, water has entered the tunnels in Hankou, and the Japanese Concession is flooded. The situation is becoming increasingly serious, and people's hearts are becoming increasingly panicked. The situation in various places is described as follows:

Wuchang 91

Wuchang was once the capital of the Wu Emperor and was built on a mountain with a magnificent fortress. It is now the seat of the Hubei Provincial Government. Because it is located on the Yangtze River, many dikes have been built. The flood control dikes along the Yangtze River are the newest projects. This year, the water level has risen sharply, and the dikes and gates are all showing dangerous signs. Previously, there was water leakage at the Wutai Gate, which almost collapsed. Summer, the Chair of the provincial government, was alerted and ordered workers to rush to repair it. On the 20th, Xia led Li Shucheng, the Director of the Department of Civil Affairs, Li Fanyi, the Director of the Department of Construction, Jia Shiyi, the Director of the Department of Finance, and committee members Yang Zaichun, Wu Guozhen, Fan Xiji, Chen Yi, Min, and Secretary-General Jiang Youwen to inspect.

American Airship Enters Navy Service 92

National News Agency's Washington Dispatch on the 20th: The U.S. Navy Department formally took delivery of the newly built airship Macon today and enlisted it into naval service. Navy experts say the manufacturers have fully fulfilled the contract.

German Representatives Withdraw from the International Labor Conference 93

Reuters' Geneva Dispatch on the 20th: The German delegation withdrew from the International Labor Conference today. Dr. Ley has already departed for Berlin with the rest of the German delegation tonight. The conference did not attempt to prevent them from leaving or to mediate.

National News Agency's Geneva Dispatch on the 21st: The German delegation to the International Labor Conference declared its withdrawal from the conference and departed for Germany because of the insults it received from the International Marxists at the conference. Upon arrival here today, it was warmly welcomed by the public. In the afternoon, a public demonstration was held at the Lusga Dan Crossroads to protest the actions of the International Labor Conference. State Councillor Engel gave a speech titled "Without German Workers, There is No German Fatherland."

East-West Cultural Communication 94

The Stocks System Spreads to Berlin. Reuters' Berlin Dispatch on the 21st: Today, the National Socialist Party in the Weilin Zhalodi set up a five-foot-high stocks at the intersection of the city market. Anyone who spreads rumors that damage Chancellor Hitler and government officials or the policies of the National Socialist Party will be placed in the stocks as a punishment.

Reuters' Vienna Dispatch on the 21st: Since the National Socialist Party's activities were banned throughout Austria, the Lower Austrian police have also taken strict measures against the National Socialist Party's activities. The bases of the Lower Austrian National Socialist Party, such as Krems, Mautern, and Stein, have all been placed under martial law. Although officials claim that the purpose of the promulgation of martial law is only to expand the powers of the police, the situation in Krems has in fact become like wartime. All stores must stop operating at night, coffee shops are closed by 9:00 PM, and the public is not allowed to gather in groups on the streets. Anyone who violates the order banning the National Socialist Party will be fined or imprisoned. All uniforms of the National Socialist Party are prohibited. Now, members of the National Socialist Party in Innsbruck are using black, red, and white roses to replace the swastika symbol.

German Government Suppresses the National Socialist Party 95

Berlin Dispatch, 21st Day: This morning, a large number of police officers searched the National Socialist Party headquarters opposite the Parliament, prohibiting anyone from entering or leaving. At the same time, they also searched various branches of the party throughout Prussia. This was because the party had recently organized combat teams, and communists and reactionaries had joined in large numbers. Their ambition was clearly to use these groups in the future to carry out actions against the government. The National Combat Team Federation of the party in Berlin was also searched by the police, and seven people were arrested. All documents and weapons were confiscated, and the building is now sealed off. According to the latest news, the combat teams have expanded to other states of Prussia.

Reuter, Berlin, 21st: Goering's secret police, with the assistance of the armed Storm Troopers, attacked the offices of Hugenberg's National Socialist Party, occupying its headquarters and branches, and confiscating all its assets and uniforms.

Furthermore, it was discovered upon inspection that there were leaks in the newly constructed embankment foundation from last year. An immediate order was issued to the Jianghan Engineering Bureau, the Department of Construction, and the Wuchang County Government to quickly work together to plug the leaks. The provincial government was instructed to supervise the progress. At the same time, cracks appeared in the Jiang embankment along Kuaizi Street, Huo Xiang Pier, and Dingjia Pier. The provincial government ordered workers to plug the leaks to prevent danger. Arrangements were being made when the Jinshui New Dam, which is of extreme importance, suddenly collapsed. Zhang Haizi, the Magistrate of Wuchang County, urgently telegraphed the provincial government, stating: "Urgent, to Xia Jun, Chairman of the Hubei Provincial Government, according to a telegram from Cao Yunfeng, the District Chief of the Tenth District under the County, at 10:00 AM today, while urgently repairing the Jinshui New Dam, the dam suddenly collapsed, and the Yangtze River flooded in an overwhelming torrent. At that time, seven or eight workers were killed, and all previous efforts were in vain, turning everything into a watery kingdom. We have reported this matter urgently for your consideration and approval. In addition to personally inspecting the situation and notifying the relevant authorities, we respectfully submit this telegram, requesting your attention. Zhang Haizi, Magistrate of Wuchang County, bows and salutes." The Jinshui Dam is related to the safety of several counties in southern Hubei, such as Jiayu and Puqi. Once it collapses, countless thousands of people will be buried in the bellies of fish.

Hankou 96

Since the flood of the 20th year of the Republic, Hankou has built sturdy flood control embankments along the river. However, construction in the Japanese concession was delayed. During this flood, the Japanese concession, due to its low-lying terrain, was the first to be flooded by the river on the 20th, with the riverside roads and sidewalks submerged. The water along the river in the Chinese district, the Special District, and the French Concession was almost level with the bank. All underground passages and toilets were flooded. In addition to sealing off all sewers, the municipal government dispatched workers on the 20th to completely board up and seal all flood control embankment gates along the river with earth. Furthermore, a comprehensive plan was decided for the flood control works around the Houhu area. The city was divided into five sections: (1) From Qiaokou to the Water Plant, to be managed by the Wai Wu Jia and Gu Cha An Security Committees; (2) From Fen Jin Lu to Chen Jia Ji, to be managed by the Public Security Bureau; (3) The southern section of the Changfeng Embankment, to be managed by the Embankment Works Committee; (4) The northern section of the Changfeng Embankment and the Zhanggong Embankment, to be managed jointly by the Fourth District Farmers' Association, related farmers' associations, and the Gusaoshu Security Committee; (5) The Daijiashan Embankment Gate, to be managed after inspection by officials sent by the municipal government. Among these, the Zhanggong Embankment is of the greatest importance. Mayor Wu Guozhen personally inspected it on the 20th and instructed the embankment guards to take their protective duties seriously. Yang Silian, Director of the Jianghan Engineering Bureau, Zhu Jiuying, Secretary of the Headquarters, Yang Dinghua, Councilor, Xi Keng, and Zhang Chongji, specialists from the National Economic Council, also inspected the embankment one after another, but no danger was discovered.

Various Counties 97

Of the sixty-nine counties in Hubei Province, thirty-five are located along the Yangtze and Han Rivers. This time, Qichun was the first to be affected by the breach of the embankment, becoming a disaster area. Wuchang, Jiayu, and other counties were also affected by the collapse of the Jinshui Dam. The situation in other counties is also precarious. At a meeting on the 20th, the provincial government decided to appoint the magistrates of twenty-four counties in the Yangtze River Basin—Huangmei, Guangji, Qichun, Yangxin, Qishui, Daye, Echeng, Huanggang, Wuchang, Huangpi, Hanyang, Jiayu, Xianning, Puqi, Mianyang, Jianli, Shishou, Gongan, Jiangling, Songzi, Zhijiang, Yidu, and Yichang—and the magistrates of twelve counties in the Xiang River Basin—Hanchuan, Xiaogan, Yunmeng, Yingcheng, Tianmen, Qianjiang, Jingshan, Jingmen, Zhongxiang, Yicheng, Xiangyang, and Guanghua—as flood prevention committee members. A telegraphic order was sent instructing them to supervise the district and village chiefs to gather civilian workers and direct them to work according to the flood prevention and emergency rescue plans of the Public Works Bureau. Yang Shengyi, Yuan Shengwu, Wu Songqiao, Chen Zerong, Xiang Dao, and Pan Huigen were appointed as flood prevention inspectors for various regions. They departed on separate routes immediately. The stipends for the flood prevention committee members were thirty yuan per month, and the stipends for the inspectors were two hundred yuan per month. Travel expenses were forty yuan per month, all to be paid from the flood prevention funds. The flood prevention conference convened by the Yangtze River Waterway Management Committee, scheduled to open in Nanjing on the 22nd, was attended by Li Fanyi, Director of the Department of Construction, who was officially recommended by the provincial government. Li departed eastward on the Jianguo Wheel on the evening of the 20th. (20th)

Feng Yuxiang Urges Song Zheyuan to Return to Chahar 98

Zhang Jiyong and Others Go to See Zhang Again to Meet with Feng, Difficulties in Disposing of Fang Zhenwu's Troops. Special Correspondence from Beiping: Regarding the Chahar issue, all eyes are focused on Feng Yuxiang's attitude. The central government has decided to appoint Feng as the National Forest and Land Reclamation Supervisor. It is also rumored that Feng, during Zhang Jiyong's previous visit on behalf of Song Zheyuan, was quite understanding of Song's mediation. Therefore, although the central government did not express its earnest intentions regarding the nominal title, it had tacitly agreed that he could take on the position of Forest and Land Reclamation Supervisor. Because of the proposal of seven measures, the key figures believed that Feng could eliminate internal dissent and were very pleased. They telegraphed the central government in detail, stating Feng's true attitude and unanimously believing that the Chahar issue could be resolved. The surrounding atmosphere was optimistic. On the day of the establishment of the Political Affairs Committee, the order for Song to return to Chahar was first announced, and there was even talk that Feng had agreed to take on the position of Forest and Land Reclamation Supervisor. According to investigations, this matter is still under discussion between the parties. It is not yet known whether Feng will cancel his title as Commander-in-Chief of the Allied Army, and even if the new order from the central government is issued, there is no fixed date for Feng to take office. However, Song's return to Chahar is what Feng deeply desires. If the Chahar provincial government is entrusted to Song, then no complications should arise, it can be asserted. Last night (the 19th) at 10:00 PM, Song visited He Yingqin at Jurentang to ask for instructions. He Yingqin believed that if Feng could cancel his current title and the central government appointed him as the Forest and Land Reclamation Supervisor, it would definitely make it happen in a short period of time. Feng telegraphed Beiping twice last night, hoping that Song would return to Chahar immediately to preside over provincial affairs, expressing his warm welcome in the telegram. At the same time, Tong Linge also telegraphed Song, saying that the Chahar provincial government affairs were only temporarily handled by him as an agent, everything was as usual, and he asked him to come to Chahar to discuss national affairs with Mr. Feng. The handover matters for the Chahar provincial government have been properly handled and are awaiting acceptance. Song believed that he still had to go to Guanyintang and other places in the coming days to inspect the troops stationed there. Moreover, the various units had participated in the war of resistance against Japan and suffered heavy casualties. The rest and replenishment still needed to be taken care of one by one. It was necessary to arrange everything properly before he could go to Chahar. Therefore, this morning (the 20th) at a little after 9:00 AM, he gathered Zhang Jiyong, Deng Zhexi, Lei Jishang, Ge Dingyuan, Zhang Weifan, and others again at his residence in Wuyiku to discuss everything. The central government hopes that Feng will temporarily leave Zhangjiakou and move to Wanquan County, thirty miles from Zhangjiakou, so that Song can concentrate on reorganizing government affairs upon his return to Chahar. Or, after the title of Forest and Land Reclamation Supervisor is announced, that place can be the site of the Supervisor's office. However, it is not known whether Feng can accept this one by one. As a result of the discussion, it was decided to send Zhang Jiyong and Lei Jishang again to Zhangjiakou to convey the intentions of the central government, explain the measures to solve the current situation, and seek Feng's consent. After Zhang and others return to Beiping, Song will set a date to return to Chahar, while his troops will be dispatched later. Zhang and others originally planned to set off for Zhangjiakou yesterday, but because the negotiations were not settled, they changed to set off tomorrow (the 21st). As for the various volunteer armies in Chahar, as well as the troops of Ji Hongchang and Tong Linge, they will all be under Song's command and reorganized. There was a previous proposal to appoint Fang Zhenwu as the Deputy Director of Forest and Land Reclamation, but Fang did not want to leave his troops. Now there is also talk of appointing him as the Deputy Commander of Bandit Suppression. Fang's troops are still in the vicinity of Zhangjiakou, and how to resolve this requires overcoming some difficulties. As for the candidates for the reorganized Chahar provincial government, Song will recommend them to the central government by telegram. Generally, the Director of Finance will be Guo Zhihan, the Director of Education will be Zheng Dayu or Ge Dingyuan, and there is a proposal to choose one of Zhang Jiyong and Zhang Weifan to serve as the Director of Construction. Also, the rebel army in eastern Chahar has recently been inactive. The Japanese army has a hesitant attitude towards Chahar. How it will change cannot be predicted. (June 20th)

Songjiang 99

The Second Battalion of the Third Security Regiment Arrives in Song: The Second Regiment of the original stationed security forces in Songjiang County was ordered to go to northern Jiangsu to suppress bandits last year. The local defense was first taken over by the Sixth Company of the Second Battalion of the Third Regiment, which was sent to Songjiang to garrison and maintain order. Today, the battalion commander of the Second Battalion of the regiment, Jiang Yunqing, led two more companies of soldiers to Songjiang and stationed at the City God Temple in the prefectural city to take charge of the local security of the county.

Ningbo 100

Yongning Steamer Robbed 101

The Yongning steamer of the Nanhai Company on the north bank of the Yong River in Ningbo left Ningbo at 9:00 AM on the 16th and set sail for Taizhou and Wenzhou. When passing Zhenhai, five water police officers from the Second Brigade of the Zhenhai Water Police escorted five thieves to Taiwan on the same ship. The water police officers were unarmed, without any firearms. Unexpectedly, five bandits suddenly emerged inside the ship when the ship arrived at the sea outside Shanmen near Shipu. Seeing the situation was not good, the water police officers immediately hid in the lower cabin and disguised themselves as waiters. A bandit saw Chen Jiucheng, the navigation police officer of the ship, and immediately opened fire, wounding Chen and knocking him to the ground. The thieves then searched Chen's room and took a pistol hidden there. The remaining thieves went to the fire cabin and used iron cones to break and release the handcuffs and shackles of the thieves being escorted. These criminals also jointly searched and robbed. For five hours, no passenger on the entire ship was spared. After the robbery, they forced the driver to sail to the sea off Shichang and anchor. Several pirate ships were already prepared there, and they shouted and went ashore to land at Shichang. The losses this time were about three or four thousand yuan from the ship's account room and about four or five thousand yuan from the passengers.

Suzhou 102

Lake Bandits Continuously Rob and Kidnap: Gengshang Village in Jiaozhi Township on the border of Suzhou and Kunshan was approached by a pirate ship from Yangcheng Lake at noon yesterday (the 21st), carrying more than ten bandits armed with pistols and box cannons. After landing, they rushed to the home of Chen Wenqing, a villager, and looted at will, injuring Chen's wife, Sun, in the lower body with the muzzle of a gun. Before leaving, they also kidnapped Chen Wenqing. They then went to the home of a Zhao family in the neighboring village of Wangjiabang and robbed them, stealing about two hundred yuan in silver and clothing. The total loss in both places was more than six hundred yuan. After the robbery, they boarded the boat and fled towards Yangcheng Lake. The victims immediately reported to the water and land police teams, asking them to rescue the hostages and pursue the stolen goods and thieves.

Changzhou 103

Cocoon Boat Robbed Mid-Journey: Lu Jun, the owner of the Fulun Cocoon Firm in Hutangqiao, Wuyi County, bought dry cocoons from the Houfeng Silk Factory in Wuxi. On the morning of the 20th, he loaded thirty-six bales of dry cocoons onto a boat from Zhoujiaxiang and set off to return to the firm. Unexpectedly, when they reached Sheqiaotou, it was about 10:00 PM, and seven or eight thugs suddenly arrived on a small boat and blocked the boat, not allowing it to leave. At that time, there was only one cargo escort and one worker on the boat, and they could not resist. They had no choice but to let the ship be robbed. Fortunately, the worker saw that the situation was bad and braved to swim away to report back. The firm owner, Lu Jun, immediately reported to the county government's detective team to arrest the perpetrators. As for the cargo escort, his whereabouts are still unknown.

Nantong 104

Clash Between Villagers and Police: A major clash between villagers and police occurred in the city on the 20th. The villagers opposed the Public Security Bureau's restrictions on where they could sell vegetables and the collection of vegetable donations and new scale fees, and they refused to come to the city to sell vegetables and transport manure. At noon, hundreds of people crowded into the First Branch of the Public Security Bureau and destroyed part of it. In the afternoon, the crowd grew larger and larger and even went along the street to demand new scales from various shops, gathering in front of the county government building and setting them on fire with kerosene. The order of the entire city was in chaos. The county government sent police teams to suppress the unrest and issued a notice allowing villagers to sell vegetables as before and prohibiting the collection of donations, but the villagers were still shouting in the streets. Wang Da and three others were arrested for assault on the spot. The unrest expanded, and County Magistrate Ye convened the heads of various townships and ordered them to dissuade the villagers, but it was still ineffective. Martial law was declared in the city and suburbs.

Gaoyou 105

Fotazhuang Village Robbed by Bandits: More than ten bandits armed with guns and ammunition suddenly came to Fotazhuang Village in the third district of the county the night before last. They searched every house, and no one was spared. The bandits robbed until about 3:00 AM before leaving with the stolen goods and firing their guns. It is said that the losses were enormous.

Zhenjiang 106

Jiangsu Province Permits Rice and Wheat to Leave the Province: The Jiangsu Provincial Government, in view of the recent low prices of rice and wheat and the ample reserves in warehouses, has issued a special order to lift the ban on the transportation of rice and wheat out of the province. The text reads: "It has been found that the free circulation of rice and wheat for mutual adjustment within the country is the principle. Jiangsu Province, due to the floods followed by the war, allowed excessive free circulation and exports, fearing that it would cause panic regarding the people's food supply in the province. Therefore, the Provincial Government Committee decided last year that the sale of rice and wheat out of the province still required a passport issued by the Provincial Government. This was a temporary emergency measure. After its implementation, the source of rice and wheat became increasingly smooth. Now that the price of rice is still low and the reserves in warehouses are sufficient, the normal state should be restored. The Provincial Government Committee has decided that from now on, rice and wheat from this province that are transported to various provinces and cities in the country for sale shall be allowed to be transported freely without the need for the county to apply to the Provincial Government for a passport, in order to facilitate adjustment. Let all counties be informed."

Local News

Shops on North Sichuan Road Reopened Yesterday Afternoon 107

The Municipal Federation Held a Representative Conference in the Afternoon and Resolved to Request the Municipal Government to Investigate the Director of the Police Station: Shops in the area of North Sichuan Road that was built beyond the boundary had been on strike because merchants were arrested for refusing to pay property taxes. Yu Qiaqing and others went to persuade them, and the shops all reopened yesterday afternoon. The details are as follows:

Notice of Opening 108

The Municipal Federation of Citizens, because the municipal government has earnestly promised to temporarily postpone the collection of property taxes in the area, issued a notice to the shops in the area yesterday morning, stating: "Notice: The incident of the Fifth District, Second Police Station of the Municipal Public Security Bureau arresting four shop assistants and detaining them in the detention center for three days, cutting off their meals, is extremely illegal, resulting in a strike. Mr. Yu Qiaqing, Supervisor of the Municipal Federation of Citizens, Mr. Hu Fengxiang, Standing Committee Member, and others went to the municipal government to negotiate. Secretary-General Yu received them and explained that the property tax issue is not guaranteed until the extraterritorial road construction is recovered and resolved. It was decided not to send personnel to collect taxes again, and to ask the citizens to explain. Regarding the punishment of illegal arrests, another case will be handled. The Federation believes that the result is satisfactory. We hope that the shops will reopen today (i.e., yesterday) to maintain their original attitude. This is what we hope for."

Reopening After Persuasion 109

The First Special District Municipal Federation of Citizens, fearing that the situation would escalate, sent Mr. Yu Qiaqing, Supervisor, Mr. Hu Fengxiang, Standing Committee Member, Zhang Yichen, Chen Binghui, Liu Zhongying, Executive Committee Member, and others, seven people in total, along with Shang Weilongxuan, the head of the 25th District Branch of the Federation, at 11:00 AM yesterday to persuade the shops to reopen. The car had a white cloth flag in front with the words "Municipal Federation of Citizens Persuading to Reopen". When they reached the iron fence at the intersection of North Sichuan Road, Qiujiang Road, and South Lao Bazi Road, Chen Jiufeng and more than 40 others from the 25th District Branch of the Federation held white cloth flags with the words "Satisfactory Resolution, Please Reopen Immediately" and accompanied them. When passing Bazi Road, they immediately persuaded the shops to open their doors. The shops then automatically tore off the notices and all opened for business. The cars passed by, and the shops immediately reopened. By 11:25 AM, everything had returned to normal, and the dispute was resolved.

Representative Conference 110

The First Special District Municipal Federation of Citizens convened a temporary representative conference of the district branches at 2:00 PM yesterday. Hu Fengxiang, Zhang Yichen, Lin Kanghou, Wang Xiaolai, Chen Binghui, Tao Leqin, Wei Langxuan, and more than 50 others attended. Hu Fengxiang, Zhang Yichen, and Chen Binghui were the presidium, and Liang Gengshun was the recorder. After the ceremony, Chairman Hu Fengxiang reported the details of the strike and the persuasion to reopen. Then, the representative of the 25th District Branch reported, roughly stating: "When the Qi-Lu War was fought, the Engineering Bureau built walls to block the lanes on North Sichuan Road and compiled house numbers by the Engineering Bureau. In the 17th year of the Republic, the citizens automatically removed the house numbers, and the municipal government re-ordered new house numbers. After the Shanghai War, the shops and residents raised more than 900 yuan to help the Fifth District, Second Branch Police Station move to the nearby concession. This is also the intention of the merchants to ask the government to recover the road rights as soon as possible. In short, the merchants should pay the taxes of the municipal government, but because business is bleak, please ask the municipal government to postpone the collection temporarily. The director of the Fifth District, Second Branch Police Station illegally arrested people this time, and should be dismissed and investigated." Jin Jusheng also reported the details of the arrest, roughly stating: "At about 10:00 AM on the 18th of this month, we were summoned and detained. Our families sent food, but the director did not allow it. On the evening of the 19th, our families sent food again, and we were able to relieve our hunger. During that time, we could not drink water. At about 11:00 AM on the 20th, we regained our freedom. When we were in the police station, we asked (1) I am not a sub-landlord, why did you arrest me? (2) Arrests should have arrest warrants. (3) Why did you prohibit food from being brought in? The police station staff replied that if we were dissatisfied, we could tell our superiors." After discussion among the representatives, it was said that the municipal government already understands the facts of the case, and everything should be sought for the maintenance of the law, and the extraterritorial road construction should be recovered by the municipal government as soon as possible. It was also decided that the letter from the 25th District Branch requesting an investigation of the director of the Fifth District, Second Branch Police Station should be forwarded to the municipal government for review. The meeting was then adjourned. (Xin Xin News Agency)

Finance Bureau's Statement 111

The Municipal Finance Bureau stated regarding this matter: "The municipal government has long exercised police power in the extraterritorial road construction section of North Sichuan Road, and the public utilities such as water and electricity can also be supplied by the urban area. The citizens there should pay property taxes in accordance with the regulations and fulfill their obligations. Moreover, the costs of all public safety and public utilities of the municipal government are all borne by the citizens. The citizens there have not paid property taxes since today, and they have never paid them even before the war. That is to say, they have not fulfilled any obligations for all the municipal facilities they have enjoyed over the years. To put it bluntly, other citizens indirectly bear the burden for them. According to reason, how can it be said to be fair? There are indeed people there who understand the truth, and they also know that only having rights and not fulfilling obligations cannot last forever. As such, the bureau handles tax matters with impartiality. This time, the effective implementation of the collection of property taxes there is for the sake of equalizing the burden on citizens and indirectly protecting the interests of the majority of citizens, not just for increasing revenue. If they claim that business is bleak after the war and refuse to pay property taxes, then the municipal government's measures for tax exemption in the war zone have long been announced separately and are now a thing of the past. This reason is not valid. As for the claim that property taxes should only be collected after the extraterritorial road construction issue is resolved, it is even more unreasonable. Because in the extraterritorial road construction section of the city, if they have to pay special district property taxes due to the use of special district water and electricity, the city understands the difficulties of the people and will no longer collect taxes. Now that they have not paid special district property taxes, the city's implementation of the collection does not impose a double burden on the citizens there, and it does not violate the principles of taxation in any way. If they refuse to pay the city's property taxes on the grounds, it can be said that they have no responsibility to the local area, have not fulfilled the responsibilities of citizens at all, and are simply willing to have their obligations permanently borne by other citizens, and are willing to be the public enemy of all the citizens of the city. Once the municipal government submits this case to the municipal affairs meeting for discussion, the bureau will explain the truth according to reason, hoping that all sectors will understand the truth and correct it, so as not to have those who do not fulfill their obligations permanently share their burden." (Central News Agency)

Flooding Disasters Disrupt Inland River Shipping in Jiangsu and Zhejiang 112

The Zhejiang-Eastern Highway Has Been Submerged. Zhenjiang-Yangzhou and Zhenjiang-Qingjiang Services Have All Been Suspended. Continuous Plum Rains Have Caused Flooding in Various Places. The Yangtze River Water Level in Hankou Has Exceeded 44 Feet, and the Situation Is Very Dangerous. At the Same Time, Several Places in Jiangsu and Zhejiang Provinces Have Also Experienced Flooding, Disrupting Land and Water Transportation. Yesterday, the Reporter Made a Thorough Investigation of All Aspects. The Status of Inland Floods Is Recorded Separately Below:

Zhejiang East 113

In the upper reaches of the Qiantang River in Zhejiang, there have been non-stop rains in the past four days. Fuyang, Tonglu, Lanxi, and Jiande have all been affected by mountain torrents, and the water has flooded the land. The Zhejiang-Eastern Highway has been submerged, and cars cannot pass. Furthermore, small steamships in the upper reaches of the Qianjiang River have been severely impacted by the flood. With the navigation route no longer discernible, there is concern that they may sail into the foothills and cause accidents. Since the 19th, all ships have been suspended. The water and land transportation in eastern Zhejiang has been completely cut off, and the water-land combined transportation on the Shanghai-Hangzhou route has been interrupted. The goods loaded in Shanghai and bound for various places in eastern Zhejiang and the upper reaches of the Qianjiang River were suspended yesterday, and incoming goods were also blocked.

Zhenjiang and Yangzhou 114

The Zhenjiang-Yangzhou small steamers of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company Inland River Steamers Bureau in the port usually have a large business volume. According to Mr. Zhang Jianfei, the director of the bureau, the Zhenjiang-Yangzhou steamers have automatically suspended their services in the past three days because of heavy flooding, with the water level along the route being level with the banks. In Yangzhou, the inland river transportation has been completely suspended due to the sudden rise of the Huai River water level.

Zhenjiang and Qingjiang 115

The Zhenjiang-Qingjiang route is the longest, with the most stops along the way. Since the floods of two years ago, the route had been temporarily suspended due to the construction of dikes and embankments after the flood. Later, because the newly built dikes repeatedly collapsed, the route could only be operated in sections. It was not until February of this year that it was fully opened. However, not long after the operation, there has been heavy flooding again recently. It is feared that the movement of the ships will erode the newly built dikes, and if they collapse, a huge disaster will result from the backflow of floodwaters. Therefore, the Zhenjiang-Qingjiang steamers have been banned from operating again.

Changshu 116

The competition between small steamers on the Changshu route has been fierce recently, with prices being reduced against each other. The price per passenger has fallen to as low as two dimes. Amid the price war, the small steamers are competing with each other, vying to be first. Unexpectedly, due to the continuous plum rains, the banks along the Changshu route have experienced a sharp rise in water levels. According to the crews of various small steamers, the highest water level along the route is only two feet from the bank. Farmers are already preventing small steamers from speeding. If the water level rises by more than a foot, the small steamers on that route will also be prohibited from operating.

Employees of the Two Routes Believe the Response From the Railway Bureau 117

Still Needs Consideration. The Union Will Hold a Temporary Board Meeting Today. The Ministry of Railways Reprimands Car Service Employees for Inappropriate Conduct: The case of the annual salary increase requested by the employees of the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways. After the railway bureau responded according to orders, the employees still believe that there is a need for consideration and are preparing for the second step. The unions of the two railways have specifically called a temporary meeting today, and the situation has become serious. The details are as follows:

Instructions from the Ministry of Railways 118

The Ministry of Railways instructed the administration of the two railway lines, stating: "In compliance with the order, the promotion and salary increase of the employees of each railway, although stipulated by the regulations of the ministry, must be at least one year from the date of the appointment or the last promotion, and must go through the performance appraisal procedures. Only those who are truly diligent, cautious, and competent, and have made meritorious achievements, can be promoted in accordance with the regulations. However, it has been found that the railway has not followed the regulations in previous years and has not conducted performance appraisals. All employees who have served for one year are given ordinary salary increases regardless of whether they are diligent in their work or whether their achievements are obvious, resulting in the same treatment for those with outstanding performance and those who are incompetent, increasing the desire to be fortunate and losing the purpose of reward, which is contrary to the original intention of the regulations and performance appraisal salary increases. Regarding the previous annual salary increase of the railway, the ministry has repeatedly stated the regulations and earnestly informed them last year. At a time when the country is facing a serious crisis and railway revenue is declining, the employees of the railway should strive to serve and perform their duties, but it has recently been found that the car service employees of the railway have taken the liberty of holding meetings and making requests regarding the salary increase for the 22nd year, and set a deadline for a response, which is very inappropriate and should be severely reprimanded to warn against this style of behavior. For all employees of the railway whose annual service period has expired this year, the bureau shall conduct a thorough and practical performance appraisal in accordance with the regulations and reward and punish them separately. The performance appraisal period is tentatively set for two times, at the end of June and the end of December of this year. Those who have reached one year or more from the date of appointment or the last promotion during the period from September 1 to the end of June will be appraised at the end of June. Those who have reached one year or more from the date of July 1 to the end of December will be appraised at the end of December and reported separately for review. As for the salary increase of workers, the railway is allowed to review and handle it appropriately and report it to the ministry for record. You are hereby ordered to comply."

Union Meeting 119

The unions of the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo railways decided to hold a temporary council meeting in Shanghai at 4 PM this afternoon to discuss salary increase requests from staff and other matters. Yesterday morning, telegrams were sent to various stations, including Zha Kou, Nanjing, Zhenjiang, Jiashizhuang, and Qiaozhuang, stating: "All council members please note that the regular meeting has been changed to a council meeting and will be held at the association headquarters at 4 PM this Thursday, the 22nd. All council members are requested to attend on time to discuss important matters. Please do not be late. Sincerely, Railway Union Council, Ma Kou."

Staff Considerations 120

The two-railway union received a telegram yesterday from Wuxi, stating: "To all colleagues in the train service of this line, and copied to all levels of Party branches, unions, sections, departments, factories, stations, and teams: Your telegram is acknowledged. The bureau's announced salary increase plan requires consideration. In addition to intensifying our work and continuing our efforts, we hope everyone will remain calm and await a resolution. Respectfully reported, Beijing-Shanghai Section Branch Office, Train Service Staff 22nd Year Annual Salary Increase Movement Delegation."

Joint Petition 121

The council members of the two-railway union declared to the New Voice News reporter that the train service staff of the Beijing-Shanghai section, the Shanghai-Hangzhou section, and the Ningbo-Shaoxing section believe that the term "performance evaluation" in the railway bureau's response is too broad. The staff of the two railways have historically had no faults, and even if there were achievements, there are virtually none that can be considered special meritorious service. It is now decided to adopt the second step, namely, a joint petition to the Central People's Movement Committee and the Ministry of Railways in Beijing by representatives from the three sections. However, the date of the petition will be determined by a staff meeting and will continue until the goal is achieved.

Dispute over Loading and Unloading at Mai Station 122

The Railway Bureau's Explanation

Petitions from Various Branches

The Railway Bureau Dispels Doubts

According to the Central News Agency, the Shanghai-Nanjing-Ningbo Railway Administration abolished the Mai Gen Road Station Goods Loading and Unloading Workers' Cooperative and transferred the contract to Yang Hengzhen. The cooperative expressed its opposition. The Railway Bureau believes that it is handling the matter in accordance with the "Measures for Contracting the Loading and Unloading of Railway Goods" stipulated by the Ministry of Railways. However, the special Party branches and unions of the two railways believe that restoring the contracting system violates Party discipline. Each side holds its own view, and the dispute continues. A Central News Agency reporter heard from a person in charge of the Railway Bureau yesterday that the case involves ministerial regulations and Party principles, so the Ministry of Railways and the Central Party Headquarters have been asked to investigate thoroughly. Currently, Li Renzhu from the Workers' Section of the Central Party Headquarters and Guo Zhongxing from the Labor Section of the Ministry of Railways have been sent to Shanghai to jointly investigate and await a central resolution. The bureau does not intend to express any opinion at this time. As for the doubts from the outside world, the bureau has drafted a "Clarification of the Case" article, which will be published in the Two Railways Daily. The reporter then inquired about the history of the Mai Gen Road Station Goods Loading and Unloading Workers' Cooperative. It is said that the original files of the case were destroyed when the North Shanghai Station was bombed during the January 28th Incident, and there are few details to investigate. It was roughly proposed in the 17th year and implemented in the 18th year. At that time, the loading and unloading of goods at Mai Gen Road Station was handled by foreman Zhou Rongsheng. Due to accumulated malpractices and repeated complaints from merchants, it was impossible to rectify the situation. Therefore, the workers were allowed to organize a cooperative, and 30 articles of trial regulations were promulgated, with Shen Yuqing, Song Kaigui, Zheng Yongxing, Zhang Zichang, and others as leaders, originally to protect the interests of merchants, railways, and workers. The original text of the bureau's clarification is excerpted below:

Handling of This Case 123

The Process of Abolishing the Workers' Cooperative and Contracting to Yang Hengzhen for Loading and Unloading Goods at Mai Gen Road Station:

On May 7th, Yang Hengzhen formally requested to contract. On the 15th, Chen Chengshi reported on the investigation of Yang Hengzhen's situation, considering him suitable. On the 16th, Yang Hengzhen submitted his contracting opinions. On June 2nd, Yang Hengzhen submitted his application. On the 6th, Chen Chengshi telegraphed that he had made arrangements with the Workers' Section of the Central Party Headquarters and issued Yang Hengzhen a permit to contract. Separate letters were sent to the Shanghai Municipal Social Bureau, Public Security Bureau, and Security Department, notifying them of the reasons for abolishing the cooperative and ordering Yuan Boyang, Xie Wenlong, and Chen Chengshi to supervise the takeover. On the 7th, a notice was posted at the Mai Gen Road freight station stating that the loading and unloading of goods would be contracted to Yang Hengzhen starting from June 7th, notifying the cooperative of its abolition from June 7th, and sending a letter to the special Party branches of the two railways notifying them of the abolition process. On the 9th, it was reported to the Ministry of Railways for record (the minister and the responsible division chief had been informed verbally beforehand).

Explanation of the Contracting System 124

The Measures for Contracting the Loading and Unloading of Railway Goods were set by the Ministry of Railways as the fifth type of appendix to the "Detailed Rules for Responsible Transportation of Railway Freight Cars of the Republic of China," promulgated on November 5, 1932. Whether this is the contracting system, its interpretation... Although the sky has cleared...

The River Continues to Rise 125

Yesterday it was 45 feet 1 inch!! People in Wuhan are extremely panicked.

We have just heard from a telegram from the Jianghan Engineering Bureau of the National Economic Committee's Engineering Office, saying that although the sky has cleared, the river continues to rise. At 9 a.m. on the 21st, the water level was 45 feet 1 inch. The water is only a foot or so away from the riverbank, and people are extremely panicked. The Engineering Office of the Association has now dispatched engineers Wu Shilin and Tang Shangsi to the Wuhan area to assist in flood prevention, and engineer Lu Chao has been sent to Beijing to attend the flood prevention meeting to discuss everything. As for the breach of the new dam at Jinkou in Wuchang, it is said that Jinshui is a confluence of many lakes and swamps. In recent years, the bottom of the lake has been gradually silted up. Local people have proposed to block the mouth and cultivate the land. Two years ago, they applied to the Relief Commission for Flood Victims for subsidies for wheat and built an earth dam at Jinkou. Last year, they had a bumper harvest. However, since the new dam was built on the old site of the river channel, it was not yet strong. Furthermore, it encountered continuous heavy rain and the river water rose sharply. The difference between the water level inside and outside was more than ten feet, and the pressure was too great, causing it to sink and breach.

rights are not within the jurisdiction of this bureau. However, the contracting system often allows contractors to enjoy excessive profits, while workers suffer excessive exploitation. Now, the Ministry has stipulated measures for contracting the loading and unloading of railway goods, which clearly define the rights and obligations of contractors and coolies (i.e., workers), and are subject to the strict command and supervision of the railway authorities, which is different from the contracting system. The most important point is that the contractor can only extract a maximum of 10% of the stipulated loading and unloading fee as his own remuneration and contracting expenses. Therefore, the contractor can never exploit the workers under the contracting system. For example, the current loading and unloading fee at Mai Gen Road Station is 20 cents per ton, the contractor can only get 2 cents, and the workers should get 18 cents, which the contractor cannot exploit.

Abolition of the Cooperative 126

The Mai Gen Road Station Goods Loading and Unloading Workers' Cooperative has been on trial for four years with poor results. Therefore, according to Article 26 of the trial regulations approved by the cooperative, "If the cooperative cannot comply with the regulations and violates the rules, this bureau may abolish the cooperative at any time and recruit other workers to load and unload," the cooperative was abolished.

Reasons for Recruiting Contractors 127

There are four ways to load and unload railway goods: (1) The railway recognizes the workers and they organize a cooperative to handle it themselves; (2) The railway hires workers itself to handle it; (3) The railway recruits contractors; (4) The consigning merchants handle it themselves. The first method is not very good in practice, and the fourth method is not very convenient for the railway and merchants. The Ministry of Railways has regulations for the second and third methods, of which the second method is the best, but it is not easy to implement. Since the Mai Gen Road cooperative urgently needs to be abolished, and hiring workers cannot be realized without considerable preparation, the third method is temporarily used, and Yang Hengze is entrusted to handle it, which is based on the "Measures for Contracting the Loading and Unloading of Railway Goods" of the Ministry of Railways. The loading and unloading of goods at Nanjing and Jiangbian stations is also handled by contractors.

Comparison of Two Benefits 128

Although the cooperative stipulates that the benefits belong to all the workers and the expenses also belong to all the workers, the benefits (i.e., the loading and unloading fees) are fixed, but the expenses are not fixed. Therefore, if the leaders in charge of the cooperative have any encroachment, the workers not only do not know, but also have no power to interfere. The leader is the foreman, and people are exploited by him. If the cooperative is managed by the contractor, all expenses are borne by the contractor, and the workers have no responsibility, and the distribution of loading and unloading fees is fixed. For example, when the loading and unloading fee at Mai Gen Road Station was handled by the cooperative, it was stipulated to be 18 cents per ton, because the cooperative's expenses had to be deducted from these 18 cents, so the workers actually got less than 18 cents. When the contractor handles it, because it is stipulated to be 20 cents per ton, and the contractor is restricted to only taking 10%, all expenses have nothing to do with the workers, so the workers can get a net 18 cents, which is actually more beneficial than when the cooperative handled it. The loading and unloading is still done by the original cooperative workers, and the original loading and unloading fee of 18 cents per ton has to be removed expenses. Now it is possible to actually get 18 cents. Because the cooperative was run very badly in the past, merchants were almost extinct, income was reduced, and life was difficult. If the contractor runs well in the future, freight will increase, income will increase, and life can be more prosperous. Although the handover has not been completed, the workers are still ordered to work as usual. However, the loading and unloading fee from June 7th is temporarily issued directly by the station master according to the instructions of Li Renzhu, the worker section of the Central Party Headquarters who came to investigate this case. The cooperative leader did not allow the workers to accept it until June 20th, when Li Jun, together with Guo Zhongxing of the Ministry of Railways, supervised the Railway Bureau to issue it directly.

Workers Not Affected 129

The contractor does not get a salary, but has to pay expenses. The Ministry of Railways' measures for contracting the loading and unloading of railway goods stipulate that the contractor can only extract a maximum of 10% of the loading and unloading fee, and also stipulate that they cannot demand anything else from the merchants besides the loading and unloading fee. Assuming that it is still extracted from the original 18 cents, then there is only 1 cent and 8 li, and the workers' income is only 16 cents and 2 li. Therefore, the Railway Bureau changed it to 20 cents per ton, so that it can extract 2 cents, which is enough for its expenses, and it does not need to demand extra from the merchants. The workers still get 18 cents, which is not less than when they were in the cooperative. Merchants may seem to be paying an extra 2 cents per ton for loading and unloading fees,

but other unrestricted abuses are eliminated, and they are not at a loss.

No Military Oppression 130

When the Railway Bureau ordered the cooperative to be abolished and ordered Yang Hengzhen to take over, it only sent Deputy Director Yuan Boyang of the General Affairs Department, Deputy Director Xie Wenlong of the Transportation Department, and Chen Chengshi, the chief of the Beijing-Shanghai Railway Transportation Section, to supervise, fearing that there might be conflicts between the two sides. The resident railway police station was ordered to take precautions, and the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau and the Security Department were notified by the bureau in advance to send police teams to take precautions. They were not used to oppress the cooperative workers or protect Yang Hengzhen's takeover. Therefore, when the cooperative leader raised objections to the contracting system and refused to hand over, the bureau temporarily did not force Yang Hengzhen to take over.

One More Explanation 131

In addition to the above items, there is one more thing that needs to be explained in the end, that is, the loading and unloading of railway goods involves the following aspects: (1) the railway's own business; (2) the business of the consigning merchants; (3) the livelihood of the workers; (4) the social economy. However, from the perspective of operating the railway, the relationship between the railway and the merchants is direct, the relationship with the workers is indirect, and the social relationship is the result of the previous relationships. Therefore, to solve this matter, we must first take into account the merchants and the railway, and also take into account the workers, and then the social economy is also included.

Branch Petition 132

The loading and unloading branch of the Mai Gen Road Station, directly under the Shanghai-Nanjing-Ningbo Railway Union, sent representatives to Beijing to petition after the Two-Railway Administration abolished the cooperative. Yesterday, the loading and unloading branches of six stations, including Zhenjiang and Ningbo, came to Shanghai to jointly petition the special commissioners of the Central and Ministry of Railways, and prepared to distribute the loading and unloading fee income themselves. The details are recorded below:

Union Council Member Expresses 135

A council member of the Two-Railway Union declared to a reporter from New Voice that the loading and unloading fee at Mai Gen Road Station was originally collected from merchants by the cooperative and handed over to the Railway Bureau for safekeeping, and distributed every ten days, with the distribution dates being the 3rd, 13th, and 23rd of each month. Since the Railway Bureau used force to abolish the cooperative, since the 7th of this month, the Railway Bureau has refused to use the name of the cooperative to receive the loading and unloading fee, and the cooperative insists on using the name of the cooperative, so it has not been received so far. The cooperative will wait until the 23rd of this month. If the Railway Bureau still refuses to use the name of the cooperative to receive it, then it will decide to have the workers distribute the daily loading and unloading fee themselves and stop handing it over to the Railway Bureau for safekeeping.

Fisheries Improvement Association Held an Emergency Meeting Yesterday 138

Minister Chen Gongbo Attended in Person

Fisheries Construction Fee Decided to Be Collected

Fisheries Federation Decided to Be Banned

The Jiangsu-Zhejiang Fisheries Improvement Association held an emergency meeting at 3:00 p.m. yesterday on the fourth floor of the Jianghai Customs International Trade Bureau to discuss a plan to improve fisheries. Chen Gongbo, Minister of Industry, came from Beijing to attend in person. The meeting adjourned at 6:00 p.m.

Attending Committee Members Those present yesterday included 139

Chen Gongbo, Minister of Industry and ex officio member, Zhou Jianying, Chief of Section of the Ministry of Industry, Dong Xiujia, Director of the Construction Department of Jiangsu and Zhejiang Provinces, Wang Wentai, representative of Zeng Yangfu, Chen Zhongsheng, Director of the Jiangsu-Zhejiang Fisheries Administration, Wu Huanru, representative of Wu Xingya, Director of the Shanghai Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, design committee members Xu Yifei and Lin Meiqing, elected committee members Wu Zhenqing, Zhang Shenzhi, Fang Jiaobo, Lin Kanghou, and Dai Yongtang, and specialized committee member Hou Chaohai.

Chairman's Report The meeting was chaired by Chen Gongbo and recorded by Chen Qianfu. After the formalities, the chairman gave a report, saying 140

that since the establishment of the association, a fisheries construction fee of only 1% has been collected, and all previous ocean protection and other fees have been cancelled, which seems to have relieved the fishermen's suffering. In addition, the collected fees are still used for fisheries construction to protect the safety of offshore fisheries. A five-year fisheries plan has been formulated and will be implemented in stages. However, a few fishermen and merchants who do not understand the situation have telegraphed their opposition, which is a misunderstanding. In order to discuss a proper plan, a small group meeting will be organized to discuss the direction. Before the small group meeting is resolved, all the expenses of the association and the Fisheries Administration will be temporarily allocated by the Ministry of Industry to avoid disputes. He also hoped to discuss how to improve fisheries as much as possible, etc.

Meeting Results The New News Agency reporter interviewed all parties yesterday and recorded the following 141

(1) Minister Chen advocated and passed the resolute collection of fisheries construction fees. (2) The five-year fisheries plan was confirmed and implemented in stages. (3) Before the construction fee is received, the expenses of the Fisheries Administration and the Fisheries Improvement Association, 2,000 yuan each per month, will be allocated by the Ministry of Industry for a period of three months. (4) The illegal collection of public river fees from fishermen and merchants by the fish industry guild was also discussed. It was generally agreed that the Ministry's collection of 1% of the construction fee has caused so much discussion, while the fish industry guild's unauthorized deduction of public river fees is considered the most serious oppression of merchants by middlemen. (5) Imported fresh and salted fish should be handled by another investigation small group meeting. (6) The Jiangsu-Zhejiang Fisheries Federation is an illegal organization that has not been approved by the municipal Party department and the Social Affairs Bureau, and should be banned. (7) There are other small group meetings that specialize in dealing with the collection of construction fees.
