Municipal Chamber of Commerce Submits a Request for Explanation

Method for Re-electing Alternate Executive and Supervisory Committee Members 145

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce received an instruction from the Municipal Executive Committee yesterday to forward the Judicial Yuan's interpretation of various doubts about the chamber of commerce election. The chamber of commerce believes that this interpretation has two points of divergence with the previous lottery re-election, so it has submitted another request for interpretation in order to comply with it. The Party department's instruction and the chamber of commerce's submission are recorded separately below:

Party Department Instruction 146

For the sake of informing, the Central People's Movement Committee's No. 3853 official letter stated: "The National Government's Judicial Yuan's Yuan character No. 913 official letter was approved, approving your association's official letters of February 25 this year (No. 3016) and April 15 (No. 3430) stating that the Executive Committee of Zhejiang Province and the Party Affairs Guidance Committee of Fujian Province requested an explanation of the doubts about the chamber of commerce election in two cases, please reply with a combined explanation, etc. This court has unified the interpretation of laws and regulations in its conference, (1) In the first re-election of the executive and supervisory committee members of the chamber of commerce, the executive committee members who were drawn out were re-elected as supervisory committee members, or the supervisory committee members who were drawn out were re-elected as executive committee members, cannot be called re-election. (2) The alternate executive and supervisory committee members of the chamber of commerce are re-elected according to the current law. Since there is no provision for re-electing half of the members, there is no need to re-elect the alternate executive and supervisory committee members during the first lottery re-election of the executive and supervisory committee members. A corresponding letter has been sent in reply to be forwarded separately to the Executive Committee of Zhejiang Province and the Guidance Committee of Fujian Province for information, etc. With this approval, a combined order is given to the association to inform and forward to the affiliated members, this order."

Chamber of Commerce Submission 147

Submitting a petition, on the 20th of this month, we received the Fifth Two Two instruction from the government, stating that "the Central People's Movement Committee approved the Judicial Yuan's explanation of the Fujian Provincial Party Affairs Guidance Committee's explanation of the doubts about the Chamber of Commerce Law election in two cases, and the letter was forwarded for information, etc. In the second point of the Judicial Yuan's explanation, it is stated that 'the alternate executive and supervisory committee members of the chamber of commerce are re-elected according to the current law. Since there is no provision for re-electing half of the members, there is no need to re-elect the alternate executive and supervisory committee members during the first lottery re-election of the executive and supervisory committee members, etc.' When the association held the first lottery to re-elect half of the members in June last year, the government and the Social Affairs Bureau sent staff to the meeting to guide the election according to law. At that time, it was because Article 19 of the Chamber of Commerce Law did not specify that alternates were excluded from the re-election, so the alternate executive and supervisory committee members were also re-elected by lottery to re-elect half of the members. Now, according to the interpretation of the Judicial Yuan, those who were drawn out in the previous election and those who were elected as alternate executive and supervisory committee members as a result have changed their positions and relationships. How should we handle this in order to be appropriate? Should the alternate executive and supervisory committee members be re-elected every four years thereafter? We have prepared a document and submitted it to the government, requesting that it be instructed according to law for the sake of public convenience. Submitted to the Shanghai Municipal Executive Committee."

Taikoo Seamen's Strike Serious 148

Public and Union Members Express Their Opinions

The Guangzhou Seamen's Branch was very angry about the tragedy of the Shanghai Taikoo Company expelling the middle cabin workers of the Changjiang route Wusong wheel. In order to make the company realize its mistake, it decided to provide strong support. Guangzhou dock workers automatically refused to load and unload passengers and goods from Taikoo's ships. Stores selling boat tickets refused to sell Taikoo passenger tickets. Customs brokers refused to load Taikoo's ships. The seamen of eight ships on the Hong Kong-Guangzhou route, including Foshan, Longshan, Taishan, Jinshan, and Jinhua, and the Nanhua route, including Xinjiang, Shandong, and Jinan, have all gone on strike in Guangzhou one after another. In order to prevent seamen from other ships from joining the strike, the Shanghai Taikoo Company is trying to avoid it. At the same time, in order to understand the truth, the Shanghai Company has sent a British staff member to Hong Kong to investigate and try to mediate. The opinions of the company and the union members are summarized as follows:

Company Statement 149

The British-owned Taikoo Navigation Company, yesterday, issued a statement in English, of which the following is a translation: Taikoo Navigation Company has long had plans to improve Yangtze River ships for the convenience of travelers. However, these plans have not been realized because the stewards on the ships have refused to accept them. The system of hiring stewards existed from the very beginning of riverboat travel. At that time, it was considered to be of service and convenience to passengers. However, over the years, the number of stewards has gradually increased, and their power has grown. The stewards are hired by the ship's comprador without receiving a salary, instead relying on tips from passengers. This practice easily leads to trouble. In recent years, the company has received countless letters from passengers complaining about stewards extorting tips, especially from the poor, and even more so during the Sino-Japanese War last year. Because of their power, they can do whatever they want, even brutally extorting penniless refugees. The ship's comprador, despite his best efforts, cannot stop them. The company initially planned to reduce the number of stewards on board to make them easier to control. With fewer stewards serving more passengers, their income would still be substantial. Since passengers have no other recourse in the face of these unreasonable stewards, Taikoo has had to take matters into its own hands, ordering the comprador of the Wusong steamer to dismiss the worst offenders, as the stewards on that ship are particularly bad. Consider the following new system that Taikoo has implemented for the benefit of passengers: 1. Newly hired stewards will wear uniforms and be supervised by the chief steward. 2. A price list will be posted in a prominent place on the ship for passengers to consult, preventing stewards from extorting tips. 3. Passengers will receive free meals, preventing stewards from extorting meal fees. 4. Special inspectors will be assigned to the ship to monitor the stewards. All of Taikoo's ships will use this new system. Unfortunately, the stewards on the Wusong steamer opposed it, delaying its implementation. For the past five months, Taikoo has repeatedly discussed the matter with the old Wusong stewards without success. Although they had seen a peaceful resolution in Hankou, it was later ineffective. Now, there is a sudden and unexpected demand for mediation in Guangdong. This matter is only related to the Yangtze River incident and has nothing to do with Guangdong. To accommodate the stewards' demands, Taikoo had already understood the matter in Hankou. Merchants have suffered losses from boycotts in recent years. Taikoo has a long-standing relationship with Guangdong cargo owners and passengers and does not expect a rift over a small issue with the stewards. The stewards on other ocean-going ships are all able to perform their duties, so the company will not change the system. However, the number of stewards on the Yangtze River steamers is as high as one hundred and twenty per ship, so it is necessary to reduce them. Sailors, cooks, and stewards will not be reduced because they are all competent. The company is changing from a system of stewards without wages to a system with wages, and it will be able to select and employ competent stewards from among the existing stewards. The company will have to pay a large sum of money because most of the old stewards are not formally hired, so they have no need to remain. Taikoo is sacrificing and spending a lot of money only for the convenience of passengers. This matter is very important to the future of passengers and should not be swayed by rumors that could harm their interests.

Seamen's Reply 150

The Shanghai Seamen's Mid-Cabin Guild yesterday replied to the New Voice News reporter regarding Taikoo's statement, saying that the Taikoo Company's expulsion of all workers from the mid-cabin of the Wusong steamer has been ignored by the party and government organs in Shanghai and Hankou. Moreover, according to the mediation record of the Shanghai Social Affairs Bureau, the request for the Taikoo Yangtze River line's workers to maintain the status quo has also been disregarded. Because the foreign company suppresses labor and despises government orders, the labor side was forced to submit the matter to the competent trade union, stating that the company's violent act was purely due to the comprador class's attempt to replace workers and collect huge deposits in order to achieve their desire to contract out labor and enrich themselves. Permission was granted to conduct serious negotiations in Guangdong to reinstate the workers on the ship. However, for more than two months, the request was refused, causing the workers to lose their jobs and wander about in misery, resulting in a strike. This is the history of the case. Now, we hear that the company is fabricating false statements in the hope of misleading the public. The main points are nothing more than the following: 1. The company claims that it ordered the comprador to dismiss bad elements among the workers on the Wusong steamer. However, our workers have no such problem. If there are any, there is no reason to dismiss the entire group. It is clearly a fabrication. 2. The company claims that the workers on the ship are detrimental to the passengers. However, our workers have no such problem. If there are any, it is due to the company and the comprador's bad system of hiring workers without paying salaries and demanding deposits. Now that the system remains unchanged, it is feared that each time new workers are hired, another deposit will be demanded. Their harassment of passengers will be even worse than that of our original workers. It is clear. 3. The company claims that the case occurred in Shanghai and has nothing to do with Guangdong. However, the nature of our seamen is mobile, and they can be dealt with anywhere. Moreover, the case was originally a conspiracy between the company and the comprador group to suppress and replace workers on various liners. Similar incidents have occurred on the Nanhua Line's Suiyang steamer, which is the beginning of the problem. Furthermore, the company and compradors in Shanghai rely on the dock's status as a concession for protection. Negotiations in Guangdong would avoid obstruction. Based on the nature of the situation, it is appropriate to handle the case in Guangdong after it originated in Shanghai. Who can say it is not appropriate? In summary, the company's purpose is only to exploit the workers' hard-earned money and fill its capital for economic aggression in the shipping industry. As for its false accusations of the above three matters and other arguments detrimental to our workers, they are all lies. We fear that the outside world does not understand the truth, so we are making this statement. We hope that all circles will uphold justice and help the workers so that the dispute can be resolved and the unrest can be calmed as soon as possible. We would be grateful.

Chamber of Commerce Telegram 151

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce previously received a telegram from the Guangzhou Seamen's Union requesting a halt to the loading of Guangdong goods to avoid losses. The Chamber of Commerce immediately forwarded the telegram to various industries and replied, saying: Guangzhou Seamen's Union, your telegram is noted. It has been forwarded to various industries. However, the situation should not be expanded. We still hope that you will value commercial transport and resolve the matter peacefully as soon as possible. Please also persuade the associations in Xiamen and Shantou. Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, Ma

Record of the British University Dinner Party 153

Lecture by Aviator Herts

The British University Dinner Party of this city was held at the Hua Mao Hotel the day before yesterday. Many British students and British people attended, and the famous British aviator Sir Herts was invited as a guest of honor. Mr. Herts used to hold the highest aviation position in the British government. He arrived in China six weeks ago to inspect the aviation situation in China. According to his speech, China has great potential for development in both civil and military aviation, but it should be noted that civil aviation cannot replace roads and railways. The three must complement each other and progress together to facilitate transportation in various places. Regarding military aviation, a complete national defense plan should be in place before purchasing aircraft, otherwise, a large amount of money will be wasted and an effective air force will not be formed. In terms of civil aviation, based on the experience gained in the United Kingdom in the past ten years, passenger flights and mail flights should be operated separately. Postal services value speed. Even if an aircraft accident or mid-way landing may result in the loss of mail, it must not be delayed. Passenger flights, on the other hand, should prioritize safety. Passengers' itineraries may be slightly delayed, but they must not be put at risk of an accident. Therefore, the speed of mail planes should be more than 200 miles per hour, and the speed of passenger planes should not exceed 140 miles to 150 miles per hour. In the military field, the air force is undoubtedly the best national defense weapon for China, but the Chinese people and the government must not waste money by indiscriminately purchasing military aircraft. The government must first conduct in-depth research and formulate a comprehensive plan on the meaning and necessity of the air force before purchasing aircraft. Without a corresponding plan and a detailed sky defense plan, indiscriminate purchase of aircraft would only waste money. Therefore, the Chinese people are advised to keep in mind that the best policy for civil and military aviation is not to purchase hastily but to first conduct detailed research and formulate the best plan. If there is a good plan first, China can avoid wasting money and easily achieve the needs of military air defense and the development of civil aviation.

After the Philippine Study Mission Returns to the Philippines 154

Continued News on Developing Sino-Philippine Trade

The Philippine commercial study mission came to China a few days ago to investigate the industrial situation. Our officials and businessmen took this opportunity to give them a warm welcome to enhance Sino-Philippine relations and seek to develop exports to the Philippines. It is reported that after the mission returned to the Philippines, it immediately began to compile a report and opinion to be submitted to the Philippine Congress for adoption and implementation. In the future, there is hope for progress in Sino-Philippine trade. According to a report from the Guowen News Agency yesterday, after the mission returned to the Philippines, there was no news and no work was in progress. After this news was published, various commercial firms in this city related to trade with the Philippines did not think so. According to the Zhongxing Bank on Sichuan Road, our welcome to the study mission's visit to China was to fulfill our duty as the host. The mission is a study group, and its findings must be submitted to the Congress for adoption and cannot be implemented by the mission itself. The Philippine Congress is currently busy with the issue of independence, and even if the matter is brought up for discussion, it may still have to wait for some time. It is inappropriate to criticize without investigating the facts. It will not only not help but will also hurt Sino-Philippine relations. There are more than 100,000 overseas Chinese in the Philippines, occupying a superior position in the business community. In the future, there is hope for an increase in the export of Chinese goods to the Philippines. Chinese merchants should strive for development and not be discouraged by inaccurate news. As for the statement that the tea and egg samples were taken away by the mission as gifts, it is even more of a lack of great-power magnanimity.

Zhabei District Farmers' Association 156

Yesterday We Heard Objections to the Sale of the Xianmian Temple 157

Since the Shanghai Zhabei District Farmers' Association announced its opposition to the sale of the Xianmian Temple by Shanghai Middle School, it has attracted much attention from the community. Farmers from all over the country have responded. According to Mr. Qi Boju, secretary of the Zhabei District Farmers' Association, the Xianmian Temple is a monument to the agricultural sage Huang Daopo and is undoubtedly a local public property. Even Mr. Zheng Xigu, the principal of Shanghai Middle School, admitted this in his published speech. It is a pity that Mr. Zheng is too enthusiastic and truly sacrifices himself for education, resolutely disregarding everything and wanting to sell the Xianmian Temple to obtain a good price and complete the new school plan. This kind of illegal action will not be tolerated by public opinion. However, considering Mr. Zheng's position, it is still excusable. However, the speech of Mr. Zhang Yi, the director of the Shanghai County Farmers' Education Hall, is very strange. The gains and losses and sale of local public property in Shanghai City are of no concern to the County Farmers' Education Hall. However, Mr. Zhang Yi, as the director of the Farmers' Education Hall, should respect the agricultural sages, awaken the farmers to look back and think about the future, and know what to improve. He said that the Xianmian Temple may as well be sold. May I ask what is the reason? Every country has religious holy places and shrines to sages, but they are all located in large cities, with a large population in prosperous areas, making it easier to visit. Moreover, historical sites with commemorative significance lose their effect if they are moved. Therefore, churches are all over the world, but we have never heard of the destruction of the Roman holy sites. Confucius temples are all over China, but we have never heard of the neglect of Qufu in Lu County. Now, Mr. Zhang, as the director of farmers' education, actually said that the Xianmian Temple may as well be sold and moved to the countryside, which is very puzzling. In short, our association and the city's farmers will definitely resist the sale of local public property and the destruction of the shrine to the sages.

Policeman Who Shot a Madman Not Prosecuted 160

Considered Killing for Public Order and Self-Defense

Wu Linqing, a patrolman in the second section of the first district in the city, was assigned to the Hongqiao Tou post at 3:00 PM on May 10th. A madman named Qi Chunpu, who lived in Jinjin Lane, was wielding a knife and killing people on the road. The policeman saw him and immediately shot him, hitting him in the abdomen, causing injury and death. The family of the deceased claimed that the policeman should not have shot him immediately and demanded an explanation. The chief of the police station, Liu Yunfang, detained the policeman Wu and sent him to the Public Security Bureau for transfer to the local court. The prosecutor investigated and considered it negligent homicide, and filed a public prosecution. The presiding judge of the criminal court interrogated him the day before yesterday. Considering the circumstances and the legal principles, the policeman Wu Linqing killed for public order and self-defense and was not guilty. Therefore, he was acquitted in court, and yesterday he was ordered to be released on bail.

Xi Longsheng Does Not Acknowledge a Poor Woman as His Mother 161

Huang Zhou, an old woman from Nanjing, gave birth to a boy 30 years ago when she was a vegetable seller in the Great Horse Road Small Vegetable Market. The deceased wealthy household Xi Heming sent his cook Li Ruilin to take the boy back to raise him. He then falsely claimed that the boy was the son of his concubine, and named him Longsheng. Now, Longsheng is married and has children. However, Huang Zhou has suffered many misfortunes in recent years. After her husband died, her two remaining sons died one after another. She and Mai Gu lived a hard life. Last year, she found out the whereabouts of her youngest son and demanded support. Because Longsheng denied that she was his biological mother, she filed a lawsuit in the Second Special Court. As a result, Longsheng provided funds for a settlement. This spring, she hired lawyers Zhang Shewo and Gu Ao to sue the First Special District Local Court, requesting confirmation that Longsheng was her biological son. After the initial trial, the court ruled in favor of the plaintiff. However, it is feared that it is not easy to make Longsheng, who is rich and wealthy, serve a poor old woman as his mother. Therefore, Longsheng was not satisfied with the judgment and hired lawyers Zhang Rongxi and others to appeal to the Second Branch of the Jiangsu Higher Court, attacking the impropriety of the original judgment and demanding a reversal. Yesterday afternoon, the Civil Court President Li Dong and two judges, Ye and Ni, held a court hearing. The appellant Huang Zhou could not attend due to illness. Judge Li first asked Xi Longsheng if he was willing to reconcile. Xi resolutely refused. Then, Xi's lawyer stated the grounds for the appeal, which can be divided into four points: 1. The date of birth of Xi Longsheng provided by Huang Zhou in the initial trial does not match the date of birth written on Xi's wedding invitation. 2. The testimony of the witness Li Ruilin cited by the old woman has many weaknesses and is not necessary to adopt. Moreover, it is contradictory, which shows that he does not have a deep understanding of the case. The old woman should be ordered to cite another witness. 3. The statement was signed by Huang Zhou herself. This kind of evidence is very powerful. Unexpectedly, the original trial judge looked at the article from the opposite side, thinking that the establishment of this document further proves that Xi Longsheng is the old woman's biological son. The role of this document is to be a contract to sever the relationship between mother and son. According to the civil law, this contract that violates good morals should be declared invalid. Therefore, the original trial's view is very wrong. If everything is viewed from the opposite side, it is even more difficult to get the truth. 4. Huang Zhou's request is to order Xi Longsheng to return to his clan. However, Xi Longsheng is still being adopted and cannot legally restore the relationship of a biological son. Even if the judgment is in favor of the plaintiff, the plaintiff may not be able to obtain legal benefits. Therefore, this type of case cannot be filed. The original trial should have rejected it, but it was the opposite. Therefore, we request that if your court believes that the lawsuit is illegal, it should be rejected. If you want to proceed with the trial, Huang Zhou must be ordered to cite other evidence and conduct a rigorous investigation before making an appropriate judgment to show fairness. Because the court initially solicited reconciliation opinions, the lawyer for the appellant Zhang Shewo immediately stood up and stated that our client is very willing to settle the matter. If there is a way to reconcile, we can discuss it. Judge Li immediately ordered both parties to go outside and try to reconcile and wait for a summons on a fixed date.

Shanghai is Dangerous Everywhere

Defecating on Wasteland Leads to Accidentally Triggering a Bomb 162

Li Bingsheng's Right Hand Blown Off, Severe Injuries to Waist and Shoulder, Still Four Bombs to be Detonated by the Public Security Bureau

| Bombs Wrapped in Russian Newspapers |

Li Bingsheng, a native of Hubei, is 41 years old and lives in the Hongxing Tea Garden on Jiaotong Road in Zhabei. He is a carpenter and used to work in Hankou. He fled to Shanghai three years ago during a flood. At 8:50 AM yesterday, Li suddenly felt the urge to defecate. Because there was no chamber pot in his residence, he went to the wasteland in front of the Red Swastika Society clinic at the intersection of Zhongxing Road and Baochang Road. Li saw five paper packages wrapped in foreign newspapers lying on the grass. Out of curiosity, he touched them with his foot. With a loud bang, the touched paper package suddenly exploded, shaking the surrounding area. At the same time, Li's right hand was blown off, and his waist and shoulders were injured by iron fragments. He immediately fell to the ground unconscious. After being discovered by residents around, they rushed to report to the 5th District Police Station. The District Chief dispatched patrolmen to the scene to investigate. First, the injured person was sent to the Pushan Hospital on Xinmin Road for treatment by ambulance. After examination by the hospital's doctor, his right hand had been amputated. If there are no other changes, there should be no major problems. There were still four unexploded paper packages. District Chief Jin specially dispatched District Member Xia Xuanyu to the scene to investigate. It was found that the paper outside was Russian newspapers. After opening them, there were four circular bombs inside without mechanisms or fuses, so they could not be moved. District Member Xia reported the facts to District Chief Jin, who led District Member Xia and others back to the scene at 3:30 PM to inspect again. He poured kerosene on the bombs and used straw as a fuse to ignite and destroy them. When the four bombs exploded, the sound shook the sky, shooting up to a height of more than 20 feet. If the explosion of the bomb Li touched had triggered the other four bombs, the tragedy would have been unimaginable.

Supporters' Association Letter 167

Briefly stated, regarding the case of the Xin Renhe ship plotting to kill the small vendors Ma Koubao and four others, on the twelfth of this month, a floating corpse was suddenly discovered in Gulongdun, the fifth district of Baoshan County. Local citizens reported this to the township office, which in turn requested the county government to send personnel for examination and to post a public notice for claiming the body. This matter came to the attention of Yu Jingzi, a standing committee member of the supporters' association for the case. He then summoned the relatives of the deceased for a thorough investigation. It was undoubtedly confirmed to be Wei Jincheng, the victimized small vendor. Consequently, on the eighteenth, nineteenth, and twentieth days, he led all the relatives of the deceased to claim the body. Remove the Corpse 168

A square stone was placed next to the corpse, tied with ropes in a cross shape. The body was dressed in a white twill short shirt, a twill cotton-padded jacket, a plain-colored twill cotton vest, flower-threaded woolen trousers, plain-colored twill willow-patterned lined trousers, plain-colored thread socks, plain-colored cloth shoes, and a plain-colored waistband. The relatives of the deceased stepped forward for examination and immediately collapsed to the ground, crying out "Little Fatty" (Wei Jincheng's nickname) uncontrollably. The trial officer, clerk, news reporters, and representatives of the supporters' association all stood on nearby grave mounds to observe. The corpse was naked (the clothes were removed during the initial examination), with its head facing east and feet facing west. The entire body was purple-black, and the hands and feet were bent backwards. Despite being turned over twice, the body remained in a crawling position, covered in bruises and scars from wire ropes, all clearly visible. The news reporters immediately competed to take photographs. Now, the corpse report is recorded as follows: The deceased was found to be four feet two inches tall, with a burlap sack covering the head, bearing the words "Great New Company" [大新公司]. The hair was sparse and slightly bald, and the head was round and square. The clothes mentioned above had already been removed. The hands were bound backwards with burlap ropes and wire, and the feet were also tightly bound with burlap ropes and wire, with a rock weighing thirty to forty pounds attached. On the right arm was a vaguely discernible tattoo of a flower character. On the left arm were tattoos of "Never part, hearts united, forever enlightened, righteous heart" and the English letters "Nmse", surrounded by plum blossoms. The entire body was covered in bruises. From the appearance, it was evident that he had been beaten before being bound and thrown into the sea to drown. Except for Mrs. Sun Zhou, who replied that she did not recognize him, all others replied that it was Wei Jincheng. The official asked if they were willing to claim the body. They replied that they were willing. The official said that if they wanted to claim the body, they should first sign a pledge. They replied that they could. Therefore, they produced a pre-printed claim form and had the five families put their fingerprints on it. Then, they ordered the relatives of the deceased to prepare a coffin themselves and take the body back for burial. The representatives suggested that the county government send someone to guard the area and that the burlap sack, stones, wire ropes, and clothes should first be handed over to the relatives of the deceased to be submitted to the court for verification.

The 126,000 Yuan Robbery Case

Another 30,000+ Yuan of Stolen Goods Recovered

Two More Suspects Arrested in Jiaxing & Confessions Obtained; Detectives Recovered More Loot in Pudong

On the dawn of the 16th of this month, the robbery of 126,000 yuan occurred on Yong'an Street, Xin Kai He, French Concession. The circumstances of the incident and the successive arrests of the robbers Wang Maonv, Huang Bosheng, and female accomplices Wang Amao and Zhang Yushi, etc., by the concession police authorities, resulted in the recovery of over 7,000 yuan in banknotes and silver dollars. They were sent to the Second Special Court for investigation. The suspects confessed to having accomplices named Li Arong, Zhang Weicai, Ashi, Abao, Aqing, and Da Luosong, etc. Details have been repeatedly reported in this newspaper. It is now known that the two suspects, Li Arong and Zhang Weicai, fled to Jiaxing on the 17th of this month. They purchased clothing materials at the Lao Jiafu Silk Shop and bought leather shoes and suitcases at the Samsung Shoe Store. Their actions were lavish, spending money like water, and their demeanor was panicked, raising suspicion. They were discovered by Li Zhankui, a member of the local defense corps, who, together with police officers from the Third Police Station of the Guanyinge Public Security Bureau, followed them to Room 34 of the Dadong Hotel. They arrested the robbers Li Arong (35 years old) and Zhang Weicai (36 years old, from Ningbo), and found luggage, clothing, and 865 yuan in banknotes and silver dollars. They were taken to the bureau for investigation and then detained. A telegram was sent to the French Concession police station, and the head of the police sent personnel to escort the two suspects and the stolen goods on the night express train, arriving in Shanghai at 11 PM last night. They were taken to the Songshan Road police station (where they were interrogated thoroughly that night). Zhang confessed that many accomplices were still at large and that a large amount of banknotes and silver dollars were hidden at No. 54, Lane 121, Chuanjiang Road, Pudong. After obtaining this confession, the French police immediately ordered Inspector Jin Jiulin, Chief Detective Zhang Ziying, Deputy Detective Zhou Yaoting, etc., to cooperate with the detective team leader Chen Guangyan and detective Li Xiaobao, etc., dispatched by Captain Lu. They escorted the two suspects across the river to Pudong, and together with Section Chief Zhang Mingqin of the Third District, who dispatched officers Zhang Deshan, etc., they rushed to No. 54, Lane 121, Chuanjiang Road at noon. They found two suitcases. The detectives examined them on the spot and found five-yuan and ten-yuan banknotes and silver dollars from various banks, including the Bank of China, Central South Bank, and Central Bank, neatly bundled, totaling 38,200 yuan. It was reported that there were no men in the house, only a loyal woman. She claimed that she had only stored the two suitcases at the time and did not know what was inside. The officers then took the recovered stolen goods to Captain Lu to file a report. After the report, Inspector Jin took them back for interrogation at around 1 PM.

In the Waters of Da Xie Mountain

A Three-Sail Fishing Boat Lost at Sea 169

The Boat Owner and Crew Drowned, Five Deaths Total; Only Two Survivors Rescued

丨Two People Drifted in the Ocean for Eleven Hours丨

At 7 PM on the 19th of this month, a three-sail fishing boat capsized in the rough seas off Da Xie Mountain, resulting in the drowning deaths of five people, including the boat owner and crew members. Only two people were rescued. The boat itself has also drifted away and its whereabouts are unknown. The details are recorded below:

Fishing in the Ocean 170

Daishan Island, which belongs to Zhoushan County, Zhejiang Province, is a small island in the Zhoushan archipelago off the coast of the province. It has a population of over ten thousand households, most of whom make a living by fishing. Therefore, they are generally strong and resilient, and unafraid of wind and waves in the ocean. Zhu Linshe, who lives in a high-lying area of the island, is 35 years old. He owns a three-sail fishing boat and works year-round catching fish, regardless of the cold or heat. In addition to serving as the captain of the boat himself, he also employs six crew members: Pan Aheng (37 years old), Zhu Atang (22 years old), Tong Chunjin (45 years old), Jiang Yifang (37 years old), Aying (24 years old), and Yao Lin (17 years old). The boat can carry up to 30,000 catties of fish. Their fishing method involves using over a hundred large nets, each about four zhang long, connected to each other and cast into the sea, stretching for about three li. Each time they catch fish, they get more than ten thousand fish at most and only dozens at least. The catch varies depending on the season. The fish are mainly sold in Zhapu, Dinghai, and Gaoding, and sometimes resold to Shanghai fishing boats for sale in Shanghai. However, the boat itself has never been to Shanghai. The crew's wages on the boat are very low. In addition to daily meals provided by the boat owner, each person receives a daily wage of about six or seven dimes.

A Huge Wave Capsizes the Boat 171

On the twelfth of this month, the boat set sail from Dinghai to fish along the coast. On the nineteenth of this month, at noon, they arrived at the waters off Da Xie Mountain to catch hairtail. That evening, during high tide, they anchored near the foot of the mountain. At that time, the wind and waves were strong, but Zhu and the other six people, accustomed to this kind of life, did not find it unusual. After dinner, around seven o'clock, it was already dark, and the evening wind became stronger, so the waves became more rapid, suddenly rising to about two or three zhang. The turbulent waves came rolling in incessantly, and the fate of the boat came to an end. At that time, a huge wave came rushing in, and the boat was immediately overturned. Two people were trapped in the cabin and died because they could not climb out. The remaining five people reacted quickly, each grabbing a piece of the cabin plank and letting the water carry them away. Due to the rising tide, they gradually floated closer to the coast. Late that night, they saw a ship passing by about a hundred zhang away. The five people shouted for help, but the ship did not hear them. At three o'clock in the morning, the tide turned, and the five people were carried out again by the tide. Three of them drifted away first and drowned at sea. The remaining two people, Pan Aheng and Zhu Atang, still held tightly to the planks and were able to survive. Until six o'clock in the morning, they floated near Da Xie Mountain and were close to the New Yangtze pilot boat, where they were rescued. These two people had drifted in the ocean for eleven hours and managed to survive, which was very dangerous.

Companions Die Tragically 172

The ship rescued Pan and Zhu, changed them into dry clothes, and gave them warm medicine to eat to ward off the cold. The two people stayed on the ship for a day and night. Yesterday morning, the ship returned to Shanghai and sent the two people to the Customs Harbor Affairs Office, which in turn sent them to the Water Police Station. After the police station learned the details of the disaster, they ordered them to be sent back to their hometown in Ningbo by the Ningbo Fellow Association. According to the two men, the disaster they encountered was unexpected. The loss of the boat alone amounts to thousands of dollars. There were also thousands of hairtail caught on board, which have all scattered. The five crew members who died have not yet been notified to their families, which is even more tragic. Now, the two of us are eager to return home and hope that the police station will send us back to our hometown as soon as possible so that we can inform the families. The two men spoke in a dialect similar to Ningbo and seemed sincere.

Overseas Chinese Merchants in Japan Involved in Lawsuit for Selling Gold Bars 173

One Side Demands Travel Expenses Along the Way; The Other Seeks to Recover Embezzled Funds

丨丨 Arguments Concluded; Awaiting Judgment 丨丨

Lin Yimei, Wang Bingchu, Hua Wuchuan, Wang Xingqing, Xu Jibiao, Li Maozhang, and others, overseas Chinese merchants in Japan, recently had a dispute over the selling price of gold bars that they transported from Japan to Shanghai. Each side refused to yield, so they sued each other in the First Special District Local Court. Each side presented their own arguments. According to the complaint filed by the plaintiffs Lin Yimei and his wife, Lin Shen, they operated a business in Yokohama, Japan. Before returning to China in March of this year, they were entrusted by the defendants Wang Bingchu and four others to carry 141 taels and 3 qian of gold bars to Shanghai for sale, with a limited price of 83 yuan per tael. All expenses along the way were to be borne by the entrusters. At that time, Wang Bingchu was detained by the Japanese police for illegally exporting gold bars, while the others, including Hua Wuchuan, had already returned to China. When the Lins arrived in Shanghai, the others were already waiting in Shanghai. Lin sold the gold bars to the Hongtai Money Exchange on Outer Hongqiao for 100 yuan per tael. Lin believed that the expenses along the way amounted to 17 yuan per tael and should be deducted from the price. Therefore, when he handed over the money to the others, he gave them 11,727 yuan and 9 jiao. The remaining 2,402 yuan and 1 jiao was used to offset the expenses he had advanced. However, Lin claimed that the total expenses along the way amounted to 4,039 yuan. After deducting the offset amount, there was still 1,636 yuan and 9 jiao that needed to be reimbursed. He asked the others to make up the difference, but the others not only refused but also claimed that the actual selling price at the time was 107.5 yuan per tael. They gathered a group of people and went to Lin's house to demand the return of the embezzled funds. After a conflict with Lin, the others reported the matter to the Hongkou police station at midnight on the 20th of last month. The head of the police sent Detective Sun Aizhong to investigate. Lin was not at home, so they arrested Lin's wife. However, after finding no evidence, they released her. Lin claimed that the defendants should not have made false accusations and assaulted his wife. They had committed crimes under Articles 180, 363, and 293 of the criminal law. In addition to requesting punishment, he also demanded compensation for his wife's medical expenses of 30 yuan. After Wang Bingchu and Liu Wuchuan were accused, they also filed a counterclaim against the Lins, claiming that Lin had committed several crimes and describing the circumstances of the gold bars being defrauded. The business locations of Wang Bingchu and others were all in Tokyo, while Lin's business location in Yokohama was hundreds of miles away. Since the Sino-Japanese conflict had worsened, Wang and others felt endangered in the enemy country, so they closed their businesses and used their cash to purchase over 140 taels of gold bars. They entrusted Liu Wuchuan to take care of them, hoping to smuggle them back to China. Lin Yimei learned of this. At that time, the Japanese government strictly prohibited the export of gold, so Lin willingly flattered foreigners and harmed his compatriots by secretly reporting to the Japanese police. Wang Bingchu was immediately summoned by the Japanese police for investigation. Lin then rushed to Liu Wuchuan's shop, informed him that Wang had been arrested, and took the opportunity to threaten him, saying that the police station would soon send people to search the shop. If the hidden gold bars were found by the police, they would be subject to severe penalties and confiscation. Liu and the other four people, unaware of Lin's trickery, were grateful to him and entrusted all their gold bars to Lin for temporary safekeeping, intending to retrieve them from Lin before their departure to Shanghai. Unexpectedly, Lin immediately took his wife and left Japan for Shanghai. As soon as he arrived, he sold the gold bars for 107 yuan per tael. When Liu Wuchuan and others tracked him down, the goods had already been sold. Liu and others immediately notified Wang Bingchu to rush to Shanghai and negotiated with Lin. Lin realized that it would be difficult to swallow everything, so he returned over 11,700 yuan of the gold price. According to Liu and others' calculations, there was still a shortage of over 3,380 yuan. Chen Jingui, a friend of Lin, came forward to mediate and agreed that Lin would pay another 1,000 yuan to settle the matter. Unexpectedly, Lin initially agreed but then went back on his word and refused to pay this 1,000 yuan, preferring to hire a lawyer and litigate the matter. As for the various allegations made by Lin, Wang Bingchu and others also refuted them one by one, stating that they were originally in business for profit and would not limit themselves to selling at 83 yuan. Their statements were obviously false. Even if it were true that they had entrusted him to carry the gold bars, how could the expenses for carrying a mere hundred taels of gold bars amount to as much as 4,039 yuan? Who would believe that? Fortunately, gold bars are still expensive now. If it were in the past when gold was cheap, the total price would probably not be enough to cover the travel expenses, which shows their psychology. As for Lin selling the gold bars for 107 yuan, this can be verified by the market price on that day. Therefore, they especially request that he be punished for fraud, embezzlement, and other crimes, and that he be ordered to repay the remaining 4,039 yuan. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Su Xiefen of the First Special District Local Court opened a hearing and summoned both sides for questioning. After the lawyers Gu Hanli, representing Lin Yimei, and Tang Huaiqun, representing Wang Bingchu, concluded their arguments, the judge announced that a date would be set for judgment.

Revival of Sanlintang Watermelons 174

Agricultural Education Center Guiding Improved Planting Methods

The melon crops of Sanlintang, Pudong, have always been renowned, especially watermelons. In recent years, farmers have been careless about selecting seeds, sowing, transplanting, and pressing vines. As a result, the yield has decreased, and the farmers do not blame themselves for their poor methods, but simply complain about their bad luck. Furthermore, due to the high transportation costs, the extortion of hooligans, and the exploitation of unscrupulous merchants, they have found it unprofitable. Therefore, they have switched to planting other crops, resulting in a year-on-year decrease in the total output. The Sanlin Farmers' Education Center, aware of this situation, convened farmers this spring before the sowing of melon crops to lecture and discuss planting methods, providing extremely detailed procedures. The general interest of farmers in planting melons has been revived. According to the center's survey, within the experimental district of three li, more than a hundred households have replanted watermelons, covering 400 mu of land. The growth is also quite healthy. Currently, the center has established the Sanlin Melon Transportation and Sales Limited Cooperative in order to reduce transportation costs and prevent exploitation. It has submitted a request to the county government to forward it to the municipal government for protection. From now on, Sanlintang watermelons will be revived in Shanghai.

Sun Fengxiang, Shot by a Stray Bullet, Dies of His Injuries 175

At 10:30 PM on the 14th of this month, after Xu Amao's home at No. 186, Gui'an Lane, Min Ti Ni Yin Road, French Concession, was broken into and robbed by armed bandits, the bandits fled with the loot. The victim followed behind them and reported to the patrolmen on Kai Zi Er Road, asking them to pursue the bandits. The bandits noticed and opened fire to resist arrest, causing a stray bullet to hit Sun Fengxiang (29 years old, from Yancheng, residing in a bungalow in Dunhou Lane, Kai Zi Er Road, working as a chauffeur for the Butterfly Bowtie Company), He Fengle (inspector at the Great World entertainment center), Ding Qiaosheng (waiter at the Yixing Noodle Restaurant), and three others. The police station sent the injured individuals to the hospital for treatment. The bandits fled to the intersection of Ai Duo Ya Road and Da Gu Road, where they were shot back by a Western patrolman and Chinese patrolman No. 587. One bandit was shot and injured, falling on the Public Concession side. The patrolmen seized his pistol, arrested him, and sent him to the Public Works Department prison hospital for treatment. It was determined that the bandit's name was Wang Jinsheng, 24 years old, from Changshu, a peddler. The details have already been reported in this newspaper. The other day, the French police sent Wang to the Criminal Division of the Second Special Court, and the police lawyer requested a postponement until the defendant and victims had recovered from their injuries before resuming the hearing. Judge Li Changnian reviewed the report and approved the request. Now, Sun Fengxiang, who was shot by the bandits, had already gone home to sleep that night. At around ten o'clock, he went out again to relieve himself in the Eight Immortals Bridge small vegetable market and was hit in the left waist by a stray bullet. The bullet did not penetrate, but his intestines were severed. He was treated at Guangci Hospital but died at 6:30 yesterday morning. The hospital notified the police station to send the body to the Tongren Fuyuan branch hall for a coroner's inquest, pending a report to the court for an examination today.

Tang Jiapeng's Funeral Held Yesterday 176

Tang Jiapeng, the former manager of the Great World entertainment center, after his murder, had his remains examined by the Second Special District Court the other day. The body was then moved to the Chinese Funeral Home on Haige Road for the encoffining ceremony. The funeral was held yesterday. At 2 PM, the procession set off from the funeral home, passing through Haige Road, Fuxu Road, Luzong Road, Ai Duo Ya Road, Xizang Road, Fuzhou Road, Shandong Road, and then turning back into the French Concession along Min Ti Ni Yin Road, directly to the Dinghai Fellow Association in Xieqiao for temporary placement. Many people paid their respects along the way. The British and French police stations dispatched police officers to maintain order. Over a thousand people from all walks of life went to carry the ropes. The crowd of mourners was overwhelming, and the road was blocked.

Guangdong Child Fooled 178

Fifteen-Year-Old Steals Jewelry and Silver Dollars

Yesterday Took the Taiyuan Ship to Xiamen

Xu Jinzhang, a Cantonese man in his forties, has operated the Taichang Machinery Factory at the mouth of Fude Lane, Hengbang Bridge, North Sichuan Road, for several years. His business has been doing fairly well, and he has accumulated some savings. He has a son named Hongsheng, who is only fifteen years old and still in school. Unexpectedly, Mr. Xu passed away from illness in March of this year, leaving behind the Taichang Machinery Factory, which is now managed by his wife. Her son, seeing that his father had passed away, pretended to help his mother take care of the store and quit school, idling at home without learning or making progress. He spends his days wandering outside. Although his mother has repeatedly tried to persuade him, it has had no effect. She thinks he is her only son and there is nothing she can do. Unexpectedly, he recently met a Mr. Yi, also a Cantonese, about twenty years old, in a certain sports association. Mr. Yi was dressed in Western clothes and leather shoes. The two became friends at first sight. However, Mr. Yi thought that Hongsheng was young and foolish, so he tempted him in every way. Hongsheng secretly took his mother's gold bracelet, over eight hundred silver dollars, and a land deed for two fen, nine li, and three hao of land in Xu Houde Hall at No. 5, Baiziwei, Jiangwan, and ran away with Mr. Yi. Yesterday morning, the two boarded the Taigu Company's Taiyuan ship, having booked cabin No. 28 in first class, intending to go to Xiamen. After one of the youth's father's friends learned of this, he informed the youth's mother, who immediately sent someone to the Taiyuan ship to intercept them. When they arrived at the pier, the Taiyuan had already weighed anchor and left port, so they returned to the store and reported the matter. The youth's mother then reported the matter to the police station and requested the Women and Children's Relief Association to try to find them. She also planned to report the loss of the land deed to the Land Bureau.

Male Corpse Found Hanging 179

At around one o'clock this morning, a man dressed in blue cloth shirt and trousers, bareheaded and barefoot, resembling a beggar, about forty years old, was found hanging inside Sande Lane, Meibai Ke Road. No. 2203 patrol officer of the Xinzha Police Station investigated and used the fire department's ambulance to transport the body to Renji Hospital, which was then transferred to the Coroner's office to await inspection.

Special Publication 187

Shen Bao Series

An Abstract of the Analysis of the World Economic Panic Translated by Lu Guixiang. The whole book has 88 pages. The price of the paper cover in 32mo is 25 cents. The world economy has been mired in panic for nearly four years. During these four years, the world has been more disturbed and uneasy than ever before. Rulers of various countries have been running around calling for help, and have exhausted all methods to seek relief, but in the end, because of the various contradictions of their own cannot be eliminated, the result is that none of them have been effective. On the contrary, the process of panic is only getting deeper and deeper. Now the World Economic Conference is also being held. However, the inherent contradictions of capitalism have long doomed its historical fate. The convocation of the economic conference is nothing more than the final struggle, and there will be no good results there; The question currently before us is where will the world go in the future? We should pay close attention to this question. Especially for our backward China, what will be its future? What is its relationship with the world economy? We should especially study it carefully. This book is translated in response to this need. Although its position is said to be capitalist, its observation of the problem is somewhat incorrect, but the general claim is fair. Moreover, we cannot be biased in one aspect when studying each problem. In addition to the basic theory, we should include the opinions of other positive and negative aspects, and then compare the gains and losses to draw a correct conclusion. Therefore, we should pay close attention to the observations and opinions of bourgeois economists on the current economic panic, and this book is a representative work. The author of this book, Dr. Paul Einzing, is a famous economist of the world, and his works are as rich as forests. This book is also one of his most recent proud works. This book was published in 1929. In less than three years, it has been reprinted three times, and it is popular in Europe and the United States. Its value can be known. The book is divided into four chapters. Chapter 1: Introduction. Chapter 2: Causes of Panic. It is divided into 14 sections, which lists all the views of economists on the causes of panic, and discusses the gains and losses one by one. Chapter 3: The Way Out. Discusses the way out of the world economy in the future, and is divided into six sections, which discusses in detail the solutions to all aspects of the economic panic. Chapter 4: Future Prospects, is the conclusion of the whole book. How can the current world economic panic be resolved? In the end, he attributed it to the close cooperation of the world to save the danger of capitalism. He has a detailed narrative on this point. Between the lines, it seems that the future is very promising. Is there any hope? Is the capitalist cooperation he advocates possible in fact? Let's watch the facts quietly. However, in any case, this book is indeed a very valuable reading from its own position, especially when the World Economic Conference is being held. This book is very useful for studying the World Economic Conference. As for the clarity of chapters, the translation is simple and easy to understand, and there is no drawback of boredom and bitterness.

National Products Talk

National Products and Foreign Products 190

— Zhou Limin

丨China's International Trade in the Past Ten Years丨

No matter which nation it is, they always like to buy goods from their own country to show their patriotism. Even if the goods produced in their own country are the worst and the most shoddy; they always argue that they are good and beautiful, just like "a bald man's son wearing flowers"!

However, the Chinese nation is very different, and is inversely proportional to foreigners: wearing a western suit, eating western food, living in a western-style house, taking a car, and household items are all foreign goods, not enough to show their extravagance 丨 Even for ordinary people, they are also full of foreign style, such as matches, kerosene, foreign lamps, foreign stoves, foreign socks, foreign umbrellas... none of them are non-foreign 丨 What is the reason for this?

The meaning is simple. The national products of handicrafts adhere to the old methods left over from ancient times, do not seek improvement, have no scientific mind, and are always so lousy! Foreign goods can use machines to manufacture quickly and constantly transform them!

Constantly innovating! Then how can the national products that "do not advance will retreat" compare to even one ten thousandth of them! How can national products not fall

miles and miles 丨 Now I will briefly list the general situation of China's international trade in the past ten years to see the general decline of national products:

Year Total number of national product exports Total number of foreign product imports Total number of international trade 12 940 million taels 1.12 billion taels 1.88 billion taels 13 110 million taels 1.27 billion taels 194 million taels 14 140 million taels 1.21 billion taels 194 million taels 15 120 million taels 1.37 billion taels 218 million taels 16 121 million taels 1.3 billion taels 210 million taels 17 123 million taels 1.41 billion taels 222 million taels 18 125 million taels 1.48 billion taels 232 million taels 19 113 million taels 1.58 billion taels 223 million taels 20 119 million taels 1.63 billion taels 238 million taels 21 72 million taels 1.31 billion taels 175 million taels From this point of view, international trade has declined greatly in the past year. It can also be seen that the difference between the export of national products and the import of foreign products is very large! There is even a world of difference between international trade! The total number of international trade and national product exports differs by more than one time, which is shocking.

Are we going to let foreign goods import as much as they want, and let national goods decline and degenerate at all costs? Are we going to allow the economic aggression of the great powers to lead to the point of national subjugation and racial extinction? Otherwise, in this National Products Year, how should we turn over a new leaf, do our best to promote and transform, cater to the psychology of the masses, and seek perfect national products!

Mom!! How am I? 191

— Ms. Hu Louzhen

Lü'er hurried back from school, sweat still flowing from his head and cheeks, with some innocent worries on his face, looking like he wanted to cry but couldn't laugh! Running to his mother, he said with a hesitant tone:

"Mom! How am I?

"Today at school, I heard our Mr. Li say: 'Anyone who buys foreign goods, especially Japanese goods, will be fined a big ocean!' The money from the fines will be donated to the children's national salvation airplane!" "Good baby 丨 Although you are only eight or nine years old, you are very able to know how to love your country; In the past, when your father was still alive, he was a very enthusiastic person in promoting national products and resisting foreign goods, alas 丨 It's a pity that he is no longer in this world 丨 "

Lü'er's mother said to Lü'er in a comforting and regretful tone; Both mother and son shed tears, Lü'er was very calm, his eyes fixed on his mother, 丨 thoughtful.

"Good baby 丨 Before, when you were only five years old, I bought you a small flower umbrella made in Japan, and your father scolded me severely. I couldn't bear it at the time, so we had a big argument! Ah! Thinking about it now, I feel endless regret. Your father's intention was really good! ···· Ah! My baby, I only hope that you will continue your father's will, serve the society, vigorously promote national products, overthrow all foreign goods in the market, and don't send the pure white money to foreign devils to use! "

Lü'er was still listening silently, and a white cloud suddenly appeared on his red face; He lowered his head, thinking about what Mr. Li said, thinking about a large amount of money being sent to foreigners to use ········· It's really good, and it's really too dangerous!

Teachers and National Products Yin Pavilion 192

—

Now that China is suffering from poverty and exhaustion due to the inflow of foreign goods, the customs cannot increase taxes as much as possible for a while to stop the endless dumping of foreign goods. Our own industry cannot fully supply the needs of our country. Therefore, for this domestic product, which is half machine-made and half hand-made, the customs cannot fully protect it. Only when the people are determined to purchase and use domestic products can it be saved.

However, the general people are very scattered. If you want to have considerable effectiveness, it is better for the teachers of all schools in the country to swear to purchase and use domestic products, and also order students to purchase and use domestic products, and persuade the people to also purchase and use domestic products. Then this invisible force is really great. Teachers, don’t underestimate your own status. You must know that the uncrowned emperor who protects national products is the teacher. Teachers actually hold the supreme power to protect national products, which cannot be prohibited by treaties and cannot be reached by military force. Even if the imperialists are very fierce and capable, they cannot interfere with the teachers' protection of national products. Teachers, please recognize your own position, recognize your own strength, and work hard to serve the country!

National Product Survey

My country's mosquito incense business (below) 193

— Songlu

Japanese mosquito incense is sold in Korea, India, and the South Seas Islands. Naturally, China, a country with backward industries, is also its only sales tail. Before May Fourth, Japan's mosquito incense sold to China was always more than 1 million yuan per year. After the anti-Japanese trend arose, the Chinese people woke up from their dreams and knew that to resist other countries' goods, they must first seek their own production. Therefore, domestic mosquito incense came into being. The first person to successfully imitate new-style mosquito incense was the Shanghai China Chemical Industry Society. Mr. Fang Yexian, the general manager of the society, went to Japan several times to study the cultivation of Japanese pyrethrum. After returning, he vigorously promoted and advocated planting, on the one hand, opened his own pyrethrum farm and hired experts to guide planting, and on the other hand, widely persuaded rural farmers to plant and buy them at a good price. Such efforts to advocate were quite successful in a few years. Up to now, the Samsung brand mosquito incense produced by the society has been sold all over the country, with annual sales of more than 400,000, and has replaced the position of the Japanese goods Pig brand mosquito incense. Secondly, the invincible brand of bulk mosquito incense is cheaper because of the savings in decoration, so people in the society are also happy to purchase it. As for the Yue Lizhang brand of Yonghe Industrial Company, the Golden Spider brand of Dacheng Factory, and the Earth brand of Wuzhou Pharmacy, the annual sales are very considerable. In addition, there are quite a few small-scale manufacturers, which are difficult to investigate for a while. For example, some incense shops in Wuxi, Danyang, Zhenjiang and other places are also producing mosquito incense. Unfortunately, it is always because the raw materials are impure and the efficacy is reduced, resulting in the loss of the faith of purchasers. Finally, what I hope that domestic merchants must pay attention to is: although mosquito incense is a thing that domestic products can supply the needs of the general people, there are still many things to be worked hard by domestic merchants. We should actively expand to the outside world. For example, there are millions of overseas Chinese on the Nanyang Islands, and they are still painfully purchasing enemy goods; The reason is that domestic products are too expensive, and they also dislike the unfashionable decoration. If domestic product manufacturers want to develop further, they should put some effort into these places, at least to achieve the purpose of "Chinese people using Chinese goods"! Especially the supply of raw materials, the output of our country is not enough. Now, because of the boycott of enemy goods, various factories have to purchase from the United Kingdom and the United States. This outflow of rights and interests, domestic product manufacturers should continue to work hard to seek self-help! At the same time, I hope that those who advocate improving rural production should also unite to help promote the work of planting pyrethrum.

Baiwei's Sister's Letter 194

— Ms. Baipeng

丨May all the little sisters in the country do this丨

Sister Peng:

Although I am a girl who is still in my childhood, I am confident that I will not lag behind in loving my country! What grieves me the most is that the general shameless young men and women only shout about loving the country, but when it comes to their actual actions, you can immediately find their own contradictions! ! ! Isn't it? I didn't know about the slogan of boycotting foreign goods and promoting domestic goods in the past. It was in the year of the Republic of China when I was eight years old that I couldn't understand the meaning of promoting domestic goods, but I understood that this was a unanimous call for a moment in the country. I heard that it soon disappeared like smoke and clouds, which is so sad! Since then, I have encountered the "Jinan Massacre" on May 3 of the Republic of China, the "Wanbaoshan Massacre" of the Republic of China, the "September 18th Incident", and the serious national disaster from the "January 28th Incident" last year until now. Which time has not been excited for a while because of the serious stimulus? Which time has the high-profile promotion of national products and boycott of foreign goods been effective? ····

Ah! My sister Baipeng! Although I am young, but when I see such social people's hearts dominating such a serious national disaster, who would not be grieved? We don't need to blame others, we only blame ourselves for not being competitive! We swear from today on that we don't need to bring out all the old tricks of "singing high-profile" anymore. We only hope that everyone will do what we can do in a down-to-earth way! ! ! Promoting national products and refusing to use enemy goods is the mission we should bear during this national disaster! Sister Peng! There is no other intention in this letter. It is best if it can be made public. Otherwise, please show my enthusiasm for promoting national products to your classmates and see if they sympathize with me? I won't talk too much. Please write back and guide me! I hope you will also be a comrade with me. I wish you good health. Your sister Baiwei's handwriting

Short Story

Cloud 195

— Liang Yiqun

Madam Wang was a modern young woman, and also a top-notch saleswoman of foreign goods. In her mind, foreign goods were always exquisite, unlike the crudeness of domestic goods, and only imported goods were worthy of being called fashionable; therefore, all daily necessities, clothing, etc. in her home were imported.

Mr. Wang was henpecked, so although he didn't approve of his wife's worship of foreign goods, he didn't dare to utter a word. One afternoon, Zhang Zaifeng delivered a set of white pongee children's clothing, which she had recently made for her only beloved son, Yun'er. She thought: When her son gets home from school and sees this new outfit, how happy he will be!

Unexpectedly, Yun'er, who usually came back jumping and skipping, was silent today. He came in, threw down his schoolbag, and pouted, as if he was quarreling with someone.

"Child, is someone bullying you? Tell Mom! ... Mom made you a new outfit, are you happy?" Madam Wang comforted her beloved son as she opened the wrapped, brand-new white pongee children's clothing and held it up high for Yun'er to see.

"Who wants new clothes? And made of foreign goods! These harmful foreign goods, I don't want to wear them!" Yun'er glanced at it and said resentfully. "Child, foreign goods are very exquisite, look how beautiful this one is, how can domestic goods be so good-looking? ... Child, tell me, who said something to you?"

"Rongsheng said that everything I wear is foreign goods, and he scolded me as a 'little traitor'; I went with him to tell Mr. Wu, and Mr. Wu said that we shouldn't wear foreign goods, wearing foreign goods is shameful; we have good domestic goods, why don't we buy them? Some domestic goods are also very good-looking; giving money to foreigners, foreigners will buy guns and cannons to fight us, so foreign goods are harmful things. Mom, I don't want to wear these harmful foreign goods!"

".................."

"Mom, why aren't you saying anything? If you really don't make me a set of domestic goods, they will scold me as a little traitor again; it's really embarrassing to be scolded by them..." Yun'er stamped his feet and cried.

"Good boy, be good, don't cry! Mom will make you a set of domestic clothing, okay?" Madam Wang was anxious and quickly picked up her beloved son, patting him.

"Mom, make it for me right away! We will never buy foreign goods again from now on. Mom's clothes should also be made of domestic goods, wouldn't that be good?" Yun'er stopped crying and said.

"Okay, Mom will do as you say, we will buy all domestic goods from now on." Madam Wang seemed to realize the inappropriateness of her blind infatuation with foreign goods, so she said resolutely; as she wiped away the tears from the corners of Yun'er's eyes.

Yun'er was happy and snuggled in his mother's arms, smiling.

Japanese Ministry of Education Determined to Suppress Student Movement 197

Tokyo University students successively arrested (Hualian News Agency, Tokyo, 21st) At yesterday's cabinet meeting, Minister of the Army Araki sternly criticized Minister of Education Hatoyama, saying that he had no solution to the problems of Tokyo University and Kyoto University students, fearing that it would cause trouble in the future. Minister of Education Hatoyama replied that Tokyo University students were using the Professor Takigawa issue to create waves and incite student unrest, with communist elements at work. He will deal with them severely. This morning, the Metropolitan Police Department began to act, and Tokyo University students were successively arrested and interrogated in the Special Higher Police Section.

Chiang Orders Emphasis on Education in Bandit Areas 198

Old schools to be restored from July 1st (Nanchang, 21st) Chairman Chiang attaches importance to local education in bandit suppression areas, instructing the highest military officers stationed in each area to supervise the handling of civil affairs training personnel. All old schools in the vicinity of bandit areas are required to open from July 1st, and the Jiangxi Provincial Department of Education is instructed to plan and implement educational objectives within its scope of responsibility, so that those who are educated can assist in bandit suppression in the future and not be used by bandits. Teaching materials must focus on propriety, righteousness, integrity, shame, filial piety, brotherly love, loyalty, trustworthiness, and the basic life of clothing, food, housing, and transportation. Great emphasis should be placed on common knowledge of neatness, cleanliness, hygiene, and the organization methods of the Three People's Principles, baojia, and defense.

Anhui Province's Method of Rewarding Excellent Students in the Joint Examination 199

Exemption from university entrance examinations and tuition fees The Anhui Provincial Department of Education has specially formulated the "Anhui Province's Method of Rewarding Excellent Students Who Pass the Graduation Joint Examination for Secondary Schools" to reward excellent students who pass the joint examination. It was submitted to the provincial government and passed at the 343rd meeting on the 16th. The main points of the method are as follows: Students who score 75 points or above in the high school graduation joint examination, and whose conduct and physical education scores are reported by the original school to be B or above, are exempt from the entrance examination to Anhui Provincial University. However, the number of exemptions is limited to 10% of the new students admitted to the university. If the number exceeds the limit, the order of the joint examination results will be followed. Students who are exempt from the entrance examination to Anhui University and whose joint examination scores are 80 points or above, and whose conduct and physical education scores are reported by the original school to be B or above, are exempt from tuition fees. The period of exemption is one year. After one year, those whose scores in all subjects are passing and whose average score is 80 points or above may extend the exemption year by year. Students who score 75 points or above in all subjects in the junior high school graduation joint examination, and whose conduct and physical education scores are reported by the original school to be B or above, are exempt from the entrance examination to public and private senior high schools or the senior departments of middle schools in the province. The number of exemptions accounts for 10% of the new student enrollment of a school. If the number exceeds the limit, the order of the joint examination results will be followed. Students whose junior high school joint examination scores are 80 points or above and whose conduct and physical education scores are reported by the original school to be B or above are exempt from tuition fees. The period of exemption is one year. Those whose scores are 80 points or above at the end of the period may extend the exemption year by year. Excellent students who have passed the joint examination and have been studying for more than two academic years are not eligible for the above-mentioned preferential treatment.

Faculty and students of the school telegraph Beijing to oppose

League of Nations Establishes Hu Hongji Scholarship 204

Select one person to study abroad every year (Nanjing, 21st) The former Director of the Shanghai Municipal Health Bureau, Hu Hongji, managed the Shanghai Municipal Public Health for five years and achieved great results, which was admired by Chinese and foreigners. Unfortunately, he died in a car accident. During the meeting of the Health Committee of the League of Nations Health Bureau last month, Dr. Lachman proposed that the League of Nations establish a "Hu Hongji Scholarship" for one person, and the selection committee will select one person from the current staff of the central and provincial health agencies and seaports quarantine offices every year to send abroad for research. The research period is at least six months, and the research schedule will be decided by the Health Department in consultation with the League of Nations. This case has been approved by the League of Nations Health Committee, and the selection and examination must be carried out this year in preparation for going abroad next year. It is reported that the selection committee will consist of Bao Qianxi (currently serving as a consultant of the Health Department representing the League of Nations), Liu Ruiheng, and Niu Huisheng as members. After the regulations are drafted, the selection procedure will be carried out immediately.

Promote the equal development of rural education and urban areas; 3. Attach importance to production in education at all levels to make up for deficiencies.

Nanjing City Education Report Issued to All Schools 208

The Ministry of Education previously sent supervisors to inspect primary and secondary schools and social education in Nanjing City. After the inspection, in addition to making a general report, a detailed guidance report was made for each school. This is an unprecedented initiative in decades (in the past, inspections in various provinces and counties were mostly carried out by provincial and county inspectors, but there have never been five ministry inspectors jointly inspecting education in provinces and counties). It is reported that the inspection report has been printed in a thick volume recently. The schools considered to be excellent, such as one school in Central University, four provincial schools, and more than ten municipal and private primary and secondary schools, were initially planned to be commended to encourage them. The Ministry of Education issued the report, and the municipal government handled it at its discretion. After receiving the issued report, the Social Affairs Bureau did not add any comments and forwarded it to all schools in Nanjing City for information according to the usual routine official document.

Summer School Not Filed Not Allowed to Enroll 211

The Education Bureau has summer school supervision regulations The establishment of summer schools by public and private secondary schools in the city should be reported to the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau for the record in accordance with the regulations. The regulations of the Bureau on the supervision of summer schools are recorded as follows: 1. The regulations are generally applicable to the summer schools established in the city, and the Bureau supervises them. 2. The students admitted to the summer school should be limited to students and faculty members of secondary schools or above, or other civil servants, in accordance with the Ministry's orders. 3. In accordance with the Ministry's orders, the results of the students' studies at the summer school shall not be regarded as formal credits and the term of study. 4. The tuition fee for summer schools is limited to one silver dollar per week for universities for one hour of teaching, and five silver corners for middle schools. For teaching above one hour, this is extrapolated. 5. Small schools may set up summer remedial classes, and the fee for each student per term shall be limited to one yuan. 6. To establish a summer school, the founder should fill out a form with the following items and submit it to the Bureau for approval: 1. Name, 2. School address, 3. Purpose: teacher or civil servant advanced studies, or student remedial studies, 4. Founder's name, resume, address, 5. List of principals and faculty members, 6. Course list. A copy of the regulations must also be attached when submitting the application. 7. The Bureau will send personnel to inspect the summer school at any time, and if there is any violation of the provisions of these regulations, or other inappropriate circumstances, it may be banned. 8. The summer school should report the names of the students and the results of each subject to the Bureau for verification at the end of the course. 9. The regulations will be promulgated and implemented after being approved by the Municipal Government and filed with the Ministry of Education.
